                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
Who Will Take Responsibility?
I was quite worried that you might get tired of the training you have received, but seeing your joyful faces, I couldn't help but think otherwise. Since you are not feeling bad, I can't help but wonder if it would be okay even if the teacher is not here. (Laughter) 
The reason you are studying here is for the purpose of the mission.
Tomorrow, I will be leaving for Korea. Ah, isn't that what should happen? So, are you saying not to go? "Yes." While I appreciate that response, it means to cancel all plans regarding Korea. (Laughter) I have already set the entire schedule….
Now, if things go wrong, I might not come back until after your 100-day training is over, and I think about that. That's why…. This time when I go to Korea, I have a lot to do. So, ultimately…. My busyness is not due to personal circumstances but because of the mission. Therefore, I know that you all need to be educated here and be responsible for a nation in the future, but I think about the important work I must do, which is unavoidable, so I hope you can understand with a broad heart.
March 23, 1975 (Sunday), Belvedere Training Center (New York, USA).
8   Who Will Take Responsibility?
Then, if you can't see the teacher here…. (Mother enters. Applause) Now that Mother is here, let's say just one thing about her, just one. Women tend to have a lot of sympathy for other women. Women and men are different. So, I talk to the women here. The men don't need to be concerned since they don't understand, but I want to say something to the women. When you look at Mother…. This morning, as she was leaving the Belvedere Church early, I persuaded her so much to greet the members here in New York and to visit those who are being educated here in Barrytown, no matter how tired she was.
Now, the women in America might think differently. American women have two or three children and go about their own way, but why does Mother do this? American women typically have two or three children…. That's the trend. How many did Mother have? (Laughter. The following is spoken in Japanese) Considering that, a mother who has given birth to many children must have gone through a lot of hardship. Women understand each other's situations well. Men may not understand it well.
So, even if Mother sits for a moment and then leaves, don't feel a bit disappointed. Let's talk. If I don't say this, when I return, it will be difficult because, 'I spoke for a long time today….' and Mother will have this expression. (Laughter)
Now, let's get to the main point. The reason I am going to Korea is for the purpose of the mission, and the reason you are studying here is also for the mission. Going abroad is all for the mission, but I think that the path I take is more important than you going out to pioneer a nation as missionaries, so even if you earnestly request it, I think it is okay not to extend it and not to comply with it. So, even if the teacher is not here, don't feel disappointed and wish me a good trip….
I will try to find time to come back as much as possible…. To come to America…. If I were to extend my stay, it would be for about a month; coming and going is not simple. So, keep that in mind, and while I think about coming back, I don't know how it will turn out. Even if I can't come, I have made those promises in advance, so the teacher will be at ease, and you won't complain that the teacher never comes to New York, so we can comfortably say these things to each other.
Let us take responsibility for the world.
Now, when I send you out into the world, I don't know when we will meet again, so wouldn't it be good for me to go on a world tour? But that is also difficult. Why? Because there are many people in the Communist Party who hate me…. So, looking at that, we can only expect that you will have international conferences, ideally once a year.
At that time, if you can't evangelize, you won't be able to attend the conference with the funds provided by the headquarters. To attend, you need to evangelize and buy round-trip tickets in that country to say, 'Go and come back.' Without that foundation, it is impossible. So, we need to have a meeting, but if there is nothing, there is no need for a meeting.
In the end, if there are many members and various complicated circumstances arise, we need meetings to resolve international issues, but would one person come to have a meeting? That is unnecessary.
If that is the case, even if we hold an international meeting, even if there are 120 countries, only ten or twenty countries will be able to attend. It could be ten countries or twenty countries. Therefore, we all need to go out with a strong determination, and you are confident in that, right? "Yes."
Now, let's talk about you a bit. When I leave, I want to ask you one thing: who will take responsibility? 'Who will take responsibility for the world?' and 'Who will take responsibility for the providence?' Let's talk about that briefly. So, is America responsible? If I ask that, how will you answer? Who in America? "Us." That's not America; it's us, us.
(The following is spoken in Japanese) Ultimately, it is not America that is responsible for the world. 
10   Who Will Take Responsibility?
And what about the established churches in America? Can famous universities, professors, or the president take responsibility? "No." Then, is there any country that can take responsibility for the world? "No." It is our responsibility. It is our duty.
The Gradual Collapse of America
Now, regarding what the fear is in the world and in America, the issue is communism. The Communist Party believes it can digest America. (The following is spoken in Japanese) So, what is the strategy of the Communist Party? They are teaming up with America to render it powerless. They are causing the youth to oppose the doctrines behind Christianity and to lose the traditions of America. Already, the churches in America are collapsing.
We must understand that Rome fell not due to external attacks but due to internal corruption. (The following is spoken in Japanese) Therefore, if we lose strength and unity, even a small force can cause everything to disintegrate. I spoke in Japanese until ten o'clock, and now Japanese keeps coming out. (Laughter)
When you think about this, what will happen to America? You will feel that the internal collapse is more frightening than the fear of external attacks. However, what is happening now is that the external attacks are coming not through weapons but through internal ideologies, and through moral decay, the external attacks are affecting us.
In the past, Rome fell without any internal infiltration, but now there is infiltration, and you need to be aware of that. You need to know that there is a Communist Party in this country. Can you have democratic activities and protest against the government in Communist countries like the Soviet Union or Red China? There is none. There is nothing. If you give an order, you must respond, 'Yes!'
The Communist world can advance and retreat as much as it wants, and it can advance as much as it wants. In America, if you say, 'Oh, American citizens! Let's go!' it may start, but before going halfway, more than half will oppose it. Then they will say, 'Oh! Since there is opposition, let's go back,' but that too will be opposed. Where should we go? Gradually towards death…. If this continues, I think America will collapse. The Communist world is the opposite. The more they are opposed, the more fiercely they act.
Look, this time when the Democratic Party in Congress said, 'Oh, let's help Cambodia!'…. In the past, when they said, 'Let's help Vietnam!' everyone was enthusiastic, but now when they say, 'Let's help Cambodia!' they say, 'Oh, no!' That too is about 200 million dollars.
Now, if something like Vietnam is in such a situation and asks China for 'just 200 million dollars,' would they not help? If they ask the Soviet Union, 'Oh, help us,' would they not help? Think about it. Would they not help? If China and the Soviet Union are in a crisis, would they just sit back? Would they support? Yes, they would definitely support.
If you see that America, which used to lead the world, is now saying it doesn't know, this is a curse. How much will they be attacked by weaker nations? If they were going to play such games, they should have never intervened in Vietnam; they would not have turned to communism so quickly. Because they intervened in Vietnam and ended up like this, now all the weaker nations are turning to communism, and that is the result of America's support. It would have been better if they had not helped at all.
So, having helped and now saying they don't know, the weaker nations of the democratic world that looked to America are now given a good chance to lean towards communism. Would all the weaker nations not lean towards communism?
12   Who Will Take Responsibility?
This means America is no longer needed. Communism seems better. What has America done? What has America done? Will God praise America for this? "No."
Let us become a group that can stand in the position of David facing Goliath.
Now, in this situation, who in the democratic world, aside from the communist world, can we trust? Who can we rely on? Do you trust England? "No." Do you trust Germany? "No." Do you trust France? Do you trust Italy? Who do you trust?
When I see this, if I were God, I would think that America was blessed to protect the world…. In the future, to defend against the communist world, it was raised up, but if it cannot take responsibility, would God leave America alone? If a nation cannot bear such international responsibilities, it is a just conclusion that God cannot leave such a nation forever. Do you all think so? "Yes." American youth, do you think so too? "Yes."
We must now engage in such movements. America itself must awaken, and the American people must awaken. We need to advocate for a movement that can assert that we must walk the rightful path. Yes, the teacher has said it. Ah, I told Kissinger, 'Watch as he shakes his head and withdraws from the Vietnam War. Kissinger himself will face difficulties in the future.' And now he is in trouble. The Democratic Party members are all opposing him in Congress, and President Ford is boycotting, and now he is in trouble. Now, does Kissinger just listen to the president? Does he listen or not?
What is the president? How did the president of this country become a mere puppet? Don't you feel that way? "Yes." Who will be the president who can shake this up and guide America towards the rightful path of the world? Who is there?
Now, the Democratic Party is opposing, and when the Democratic Party says something, they lose to the Democratic Party, and then they switch to the Republican Party, and back and forth, and if this continues, they will all become powerless. This has become like a rotten stick. What can be done in such America?
As the regime changes more and more, do you think America can develop, or do you think it will decline? "I think it will decline." You need to understand that you are in a crisis, a crisis. You must realize that America's crisis is right before us today.
Therefore, we have the responsibility to raise a new awakening before the officials of the American government and the American people. Who will do that? Only we can. So, do we think we can do that? "Yes." What power do you have? What power do you have? Can you control a state? Can you just say, 'Let's do this' in a few states in the East? Can you do that? "Yes." How? "Father…." But even Father cannot do it. Without a foundation…. Did God let the Israelites kill Jesus for no reason? You need to understand that without a foundation, nothing can be done. Did Jesus die on the cross for no reason? Did he die on the cross without a foundation? "No." He could not do it because there was no foundation.
Can you do it without a foundation? "No." Then if you cannot do it, can the teacher do it? "No." What about God? "He cannot do it." So the question is how quickly we can lay this foundation. This is what God urgently demands, and this is what the teacher urgently demands. We must realize that we are caught in a destiny that must be urgently resolved.
So, what should we do? Who will take responsibility? If the Unification Church does not take responsibility, we can try again, but if we say we will take responsibility and step forward, it will be the last time. Ultimately, who will take responsibility? Who will take responsibility? "Not at all…." Then will that be enough? Can that be done? If no one can take responsibility, who will take responsibility?
14   Who Will Take Responsibility?
How will this be handled? Will it fail? Is it saying to completely break God's will? 
That is why the conclusion is that there must be a group that can stand in the same position as David against Goliath. It’s not just words. It’s not just words. It’s not merely to give you some inspiration or advice. We must feel that this is the truth. 
Let’s work for three years with the heart of ‘I am the only one left.’ 
All the American youth… Do you think that youth can save America? “Yes.” With that youth? Those people will run away if they hear gunfire on the street. There’s no room for thinking about justice. Recently, there was a fight in New York between whites and blacks, and while the blacks gathered all at once, the whites ran away all at once. You need to understand that. 
For 6,000 years, God has come to America to conclude one purpose. How pitiful it is for God to have to despair again through this America. But why does the established church, why do various religions not even dream of it, while the Unification Church has to suffer? Why? Why? Why do we have to suffer for this country, to save America? Why do we have to do this? 
Why is that? Is it because we need money? Is it because we need power? What is it that makes us do this? What do we need? What is it? What is our purpose? It is not that God needs worldly nations. What God needs is a person who can fulfill His will, a nation that can fulfill His will. 
So why does God need Reverend Moon of the Unification Church? Why does He need him? Is it because of his good looks? “No.” For what reason? Does he have any global knowledge? He has nothing. Does he have power? Does he have money? He has nothing. 
15 
Nothing at all. Nothing. But because he knows God's will and is willing to fulfill it with his life, that is why God holds on to him. He is holding on to me. Outside of that, there is nothing. 
Do I need you because I want to take your money? Do I want to gain power? There is nothing like that. The tiny heart that wants to serve God's will is more necessary and stronger than any American power, and that is why I need you. 
I need you. 
So why do you eat? Do you eat to live? It is for this purpose. What is the reason for my work? Is it to eat? It is for this purpose. And why do I die? I die for this purpose with all my life. That is why God needs us. Do you understand? “Yes.” 
Now, if God looks at this world in a time when no one can be trusted… When He looks at these pitiful beings with eyes wide open, we must understand the shocking fact that the failed God is placing hope on these pitiful beings. To abandon America, to abandon the Christianity that moves America? How pitiful is God? How miserable is God? 
That is why I feel ashamed to pray to that God and say, “Father!” I cannot pray to a God like that. I cannot even ask Him for help. What if we cooperate this time and then after finding the world, there is a possibility of betraying God again? Isn’t there a possibility? 
Think about that. How pitiful God is. ‘I cannot be like that.’ This thought should not be absent. The prayer of Elijah, who stood alone at the end after being surrounded by the Baal gods, saying, ‘I am the only one left,’ must be felt. Do you feel that? “Yes.” 
You must realize that if you do not become the kind of people who can swear, “I cannot fail here, I cannot fall. I will go again.” 
If you have even a heart that can pray, say, “Please extend this time a little longer, extend it. If it can be extended from three years to seven years, please extend it…” I asked the heads of certain organizations when I went to Korea last time, “For these three years, somehow push through the situation in Korea.” So, America must make a decision in three years. We must not fail to prepare in these three years. 
Now, can we do the work that this country cannot do, that this government cannot do in three years? These crazy people… Can we do it? Will we do it? “Yes.” We cannot do it with just our strength. That is why we must think about one thing here: we need young people who have a stronger faith than anyone who risked their lives to seek freedom of faith at the time of America’s founding and who are determined to fulfill God’s will. 
That is why I said, “God! Please wait for three years! Even if I cannot do it, I will at least lay a foundation.” That is why I gathered you here after three years. So, do you know that you are the gathered group? “Yes.” Then, what will you do here? Will you return to your hometown, towards the new frontier of America, to break through the place where drugs are rampant and where Satan and communism swarm? What will you do? With my right hand, I must hold back communism, with my left hand, I must stop the youth from drugs, with my heart, I must defend the established church, and with my actions, I must move God. This is the kind of thinking we must have. Do you understand? “Yes.” Do you recognize yourselves as qualified to do that? “Yes.” You are lacking. You are lacking. When you think of this, say, “If I have a few months, I will study all of this. That time is right now!” 
Now, if you are like that, say, “The sky of Barrytown, the nature of Barrytown, let me discover a new me in my lifetime, and let me create a new me through a natural environment. Just wait and see! Within three years, I will become someone.” You must be in a position to make such a resolution. “I will not just die. I will not just die. Just wait and see.” You must make such a resolution. Do you understand? “Yes.” Have I made such a resolution, or will I? “I have.” Let’s see a show of hands from those who have made that decision. Put your hands down. If you go with that mindset and Satan says, “You brat! You brat!” and tries to stop you, what will you do? Will you push through like a tank? “Yes.” I like tanks. If you push through with a tank, no one can stop you. Did you see that? Can you do that? “Yes.” Do you have the strength to do that? “Yes.” You must have that kind of mindset. 
Persecution is valuable because it exists.
Now, look at yourself, look at yourself. I hear various reports that NBC is doing this and that, that they are conspiring to systematically drive out Reverend Moon of the Unification Church, that someone is opposing, that the FBI is opposing, that the CIA is opposing, that members of Congress are opposing, and I am hearing all sorts of complicated information. Will I work for what they give? “No.” So, I wish I could weigh 200 pounds or 300 pounds. (Laughter) That’s just the wind blowing. When a car goes fast, it meets the wind. That’s the natural principle. So, you must understand that the wind blowing is a natural principle. When a car goes fast, the wind blows, right? It rushes in. It’s the same. 
So, will you just stand still when you are facing a strong wind, or will you run? “I will run.” That’s the problem. There is persecution, right? It is valuable because there is persecution. What value is there without persecution? You must understand that I was born for that purpose and that I know that will, so I will clash once. I will strike once. Just like David struck Goliath. Will you try it? “Yes.” 
Look at your fists. With that small, delicate fist, think that you will break through with strength and if it doesn’t work, think, “Ah! My spirit was lacking.” You must think like that, not that it didn’t work because it was delicate. You must think, “My spirit is lacking. My faith is lacking. I am lacking.” You must not say that this is lacking. You must say that my spirit is lacking, my faith is lacking, my training is lacking, but it is not that it cannot be done. Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.” 
You can’t evangelize? What cannot be done is due to lack of skill and lack of faith… If it doesn’t work with sincerity once, you must repeat it stronger two, three, four times. If it doesn’t work, keep going until it does… That is why do not lose heart, do not lose heart. The one who loses heart is the biggest loser. Do you have confidence that you can influence a state when you go out to evangelize? “I have no problem influencing a state. I have no problem influencing a nation.” You must have that kind of confidence first. Do you have confidence? “Yes.” 
Then why did you gather so many people? If there were just 50 of you, you could take responsibility for all of America. Then, send everyone away except for 50! If you have confidence, this is too many. Send them all back. “No.” What will you do then? Will you go two by two to one place? Three by three? Four by four? What will you do? If I take responsibility alone, I should not want anyone to come. Isn’t this too many? What is so many? Even if the remaining people come to each of the 50 states, think, “Come to watch me fight. Come to watch. Come to learn what I am doing. You are coming to learn.” Think like that. “Why did you come? You came to learn from me, to follow what I do, right?” Think like that. Is everyone like that? “Yes.” If you are a man, you must have that kind of thought. If not, you should be kicked out. Don’t men have that kind of ambition? Is that right? “Yes.” Just wait and see. 
Yes, women are there to watch. Since women like to watch, let them watch. “No.” Then what will you do? Will you kick men out? Will you kick men out and take responsibility? “Yes.” Trust in this fist! Do you have confidence? “Yes.” When a man’s voice and a woman’s voice meet, a man will say, “What-ya?” (In a deep, loud male voice) and women will say, “What-ya?” (In a soft, high-pitched female voice). (Laughter) When you give a shout, it is hard, isn’t it? That’s a woman. “No.” 
Then what is a man? That is why men should stand firm. (Laughter) Then will men say, “Come on.” and yield to women and be happy? Will they yield to women? “No.” (Laughter) Just by hearing the voice, you can tell it is definitely softer. So, what is a man now? Do you think God would like a man who yields to women? I myself would not like it, so what would God like? We must establish the authority of man. We must establish the authority of man. We must never yield to women. 
Let’s work with a new resolution.
Now, knowing that, let’s make a new resolution. “Hey! Since I was born like this, let’s try it! Let’s try it! Let’s put in the effort and try it! Let’s go out and try it!” Women should do the same. We must do that to not lose. Our women may yield to our men, but whoever rules the nation in the satanic world, no matter how much of a champion they are, they must be able to block with the left foot without using the right foot. That must be the case. A woman who yields to the men of this world must not return. I will not send such a person to my in-laws, and I will not let them participate in a joint wedding. 
So, no matter where you go in America, men can win, and women can win anywhere in the world! Do you have confidence? “Yes.” Yes. “Yes!” Wow! (Laughter) You lose to me. You must not lose to me in your answers. When you take the test, you should push me aside and go. Why can’t you do that? It’s a fight. What’s the problem with me being the teacher? That’s good. Why? Because that way, victory will come quickly… Victory will be ours. 
Now, when you run, if I am in front of you, do not look at me, close your eyes and run. That’s good. And when I come around, think, “Why is he coming around? What does he want? He doesn’t need to come. I don’t need a supervisor or a director… I will do it all by myself…” You must have that kind of thought. And don’t say, “I waited a month for the money to come from the headquarters, but it hasn’t come.” Don’t say that. Money will come if it comes, and if it doesn’t, it doesn’t… You must have the confidence that you can earn and use money. “Whose cooperation do I need? I will do it all by myself!” You must have that kind of confidence. 
Now, if the headquarters sends some money, you must take several times that amount and go back to the headquarters clean… Pray to God and start. Can you do that? “Yes.” Hmm! I like such people. Do you? “We like them.” Do I like you? “Yes!” Yes? “Yes.” I like you too. (Laughter) 
So, why am I taking this time to say these things when I am not with you? You must have strength in your lower abdomen. Has that happened? “Yes.” (Laughter) Is there anyone dozing off? “Teacher, don’t talk in your sleep! I’m going to sleep.” Is there anyone sleeping? Is there anyone? Did everyone understand? Check if there is anyone next to you. Is there anyone? “No.” 
Then, I feel good. I feel good because everyone heard it. Shall we stop and conclude? “No.” You didn’t eat breakfast, did you? “No.” Then, you should have the composure to say, “Teacher, that’s good. I understand. You don’t need to conclude; I already understand your conclusion. Please stop.” (Cheers, applause) If you think like that, how wonderful would that be? “That’s right! That’s right!” (Laughter) If I teach you all this and send you off, that’s a zero. 
( Laughter) If you leave with a zero, what is that? 
Responsibility starts from one.
So, what is the title of today’s message? It is “Who Will Take Responsibility?” Who will take responsibility? Me? “Yes.” You? “Yes.” Then, give America to me! God! Give America to me! Let’s pray like that. “God! Give Asia to me! But I must not die at the age of 80. If you let me live until 90, I will surely do it.” If that happens, will God say, “Oh, let’s do that!” or “No, that won’t do!”? “He will say, ‘Let’s do that.’” “If God takes me away, it will be a huge loss.”
"Having that kind of self will lead to a long life. You want to live long, right? "Yes." 

Then where do you want to take responsibility? That's something each of you should decide. Can you take that responsibility all at once by saying, 'Hey! Asia, let's do it!'? You have to start from one. You need to occupy everything in Asia from there. Can you occupy it just by sitting still? "No." Where do you start? You start from one. You start from one, from one. If you evangelize one person, you should say, 'Through me, I will go to Asia! Through this family, I will go to Asia! Through this country, I will go to Asia!' That's how it should be.

Then what will you do when you go to that country? Do you think God will listen if you say, 'God! God! Please send me!'? Wouldn't that upset God? 'God!' 'Why?' 'I need to go to South America.... This country needs me, so please help.' Then He will help you. As far as I know, God likes such people. Do you all like such people? "Yes." It's the same. So, do you have worries in your heart? "No." I will do it with my own hands in South America, in Africa, in Asia! Even if I'm a woman, I will do it! How good does that feel? Now, when there is persecution, if you say, 'Oh, it's hard to deal with persecution in this environment,' what is that? What will you do? At the very least....

Would God prefer you to think big or think small? Even if your desires are big, you should do small things beautifully.

Think about it. How many people are managing the world? Only about ten people are managing the world. You should have the thought that 'I can do that. If a few of us align our hearts with the teacher, it's just a matter of time before we can manage the world.' 

Now, when the teacher came to America, did he think, 'Oh! America, with 220 million people, the world's number one cultural country, an advanced country with lots of money! There's the FBI, the CIA, and it's a den of opposition against established churches. Oh, how can I...'? Did he think like that? Did he think, 'This damn America! This damn America!'? Think about how he started. Now he's famous, right? He appears in 'Time' magazine alongside famous people like Kissinger and Ford, and Reverend Moon is included there too. (Applause) It matched perfectly with the teacher's plan. It matched perfectly with the plan. (Laughter)

Now, think about it. If people like you become a hundred thousand or a million, what will happen to America? What do you think will happen to America? Think about it. I believe that. If our Unification Church girls had not had the blessing marriage this time, they would have been the ones saying, 'I will become the First Lady of the United States.' They would have rejected being the wives of senators. Since the teacher married them, they have no choice. Is that true? "Yes." But (the rest is spoken in English) the teacher has married many people. They will comply with that, right? "Yes." Hehehe. Is that right? "Yes."

Think about how you will handle these women in the future. How will you send these women off to marriage? Since your mothers and fathers, your uncles cannot send them off, I will manage and send them off. (Laughter) Think about how wonderful that idea is. So, why complain when I do it for you? You should think like that. With plenty of leisure... The teacher went to prison in shackles, went to the courtroom, and received a sentence... The sound of the shackles still hasn't been forgotten. When someone opposes him in a sermon, does the teacher say, 'Oh!'? Does he try to run away, or is he more composed? What do you think?

If you just try to evangelize, there are countless ways to do it. 

At places like Berkeley University, they had planned to kick me out, but my strategy completely outsmarted them. I knew they had planned to finish it within ten minutes by gathering a crowd. They couldn't go beyond ten minutes because they had planned to oppose in this way, and if it went beyond ten minutes, they would fall into my strategy; I had already calculated everything. So, they came in, making all sorts of noises, but I said, 'Go ahead.' How much more fun is that than a lecture! So, I also laughed, ha ha ha. 'Do it again!' Hehehe! (Laughter) Let's do it again! Then the audience would all laugh. 'Haha... Reverend Moon is good at this.' They would applaud. (Laughter) After about ten minutes, there would be nothing left to do. They had already done everything they planned, so it was all over. Now, if they want to do something again, they have to go back and discuss, 'What should we do!' and repeat it, but they can't do that. Those who think like that are already aware of everything. How fun is that? Do you think like that too? Why do you think it's difficult?

There are countless ways to evangelize. Do you just need to give a principle lecture? You can play the trumpet, or you can fight on the street. Fighting is evangelism. By doing that, you can gather people and show them what they did wrong... 'I was wrong, wasn't I?' Present evidence based on justice, and people should live for justice. Debt

<Words> No one in this world wishes to be in debt. However, during our lifetime, we must incur debts to our nation, society, family, or friends, and we realize that we cannot live without incurring debts in various fields.

Humans who must incur debts and repay them
Just as it is in human society, when we look at the providential will, we must understand that whether it is God, or an individual, or the Unification Church, or Korea, or any country, we all stand in a position of owing debts throughout history.

Who owes more debts, and who repays them? If someone has incurred a lot of debt, and if that person can take responsibility and repay it, then that person may establish their dignity and face in society. However, if they owe debts but evade responsibility or oppose the circumstances, they will inevitably face criticism as a member of society and will be diminished in the relative social context.

In the same way, when we look at the situation centered on God, we must consider how much debt the Republic of Korea has incurred before God throughout history. Furthermore, when we look at Korea, we must also consider how much debt it has incurred before the Asian empires. If there is a sovereign governing that country, that sovereign has a responsibility to love the people like a parent and to leave something for the citizens, but if they fail to do that and instead find themselves in a position of being indebted to the people, that too can be considered a debt. The citizens are no different in this regard.

When we look at it this way, we cannot escape the historical connections of incurring and repaying debts in relative relationships, whether they are sequential or hierarchical.

Humans indebted before God
From this perspective, when we consider the issue of God and the nation, what is the standard of the restoration providence today, and where is it headed? The initial desired standard is not the nation itself. Of course, the goal is to find the nation through the individual and the family, but the primary concern regarding humanity is the relationship between me and God.

As you know, the salvation providence is the restoration providence. In other words, the restoration providence is about returning to the position that was not fallen. To return to that position, it is not just a matter of going back; it requires going through the process of re-creation. To undergo the process of re-creation, it cannot be done haphazardly; we must apply the principles and laws that were used in the original creation; otherwise, the results of re-creation will not manifest.

From this perspective, if we look at the self that is ‘me,’ we find that we are descendants of the fall. Then, until the fall, how much effort did God put into the creation of our human ancestors, Adam and Eve? If God exerted effort, then He must have poured out all His love, intellect, and everything He possessed into creating Adam and Eve as His sons and daughters. It is certain that God invested all the good things into those children.

When we consider this, the fact that Adam, that son, fell represents a loss for God. If everything of value that He invested up to that point was severed, then someone must take responsibility for the corresponding, truly valuable loss. Who should take responsibility? It should not be God, but rather humans who have made the mistake. However, if humans are in a position where they cannot take responsibility, what should be done? This is the problem. When humans cannot take responsibility, then God must take responsibility.

Even before the fall, if we consider all that is precious, we find that humanity owed a debt to God. The fact that humanity fell caused a shocking loss before God. The position of the children that God had longed for could turn into a curse and resentment. The desire to bless could turn into a rage that negates everything and wishes to destroy it immediately.

The salvation providence is a game to find just one Adam
Then, without suppressing such feelings and going through the process of recovering them, there would be no path for the re-creation history or the salvation providence. It is unthinkable that God, with a heart full of resentment and grievance, would seek to save humanity. To extend the hand of the salvation providence, God must resolve to embody the desires and hopes of creation; without this internal process, human salvation would be difficult. This is something you can feel through your own experiences with your children.

When we think of the place where the purpose of the salvation providence can manifest, it cannot be said that the will of the salvation providence was fulfilled without any thought. There must have been a process of twists and turns, overcoming the circumstances of those twists and turns, digesting them, and presenting new hope before humanity in order to initiate the salvation providence.

For this reason, it is certain that God must have gone through a process of transformation internally as the God of creation. Considering that this leads to the restoration of the individual, family, nation, and world, from a providential perspective, we see that God has established numerous external religions up to this point. What is the purpose of this? It is to gather all the elements spread out among those religions to create one ideal Adam.

Whether it is Christianity, Confucianism, or any historically renowned religion, they all aim to extract the value of one original, unfallen person from there. When we consider the countless values of religions compared to the one ideal human who has not fallen, namely the completed Adam and Eve, which holds more value? The unfallen original Adam is of greater value. Ultimately, religions exist to recreate Adam. That Adam is the Messiah.

From this perspective, to send that one Messiah to this earth, how much has humanity suffered and struggled through twists and turns since the fall? How much has God endured while facing the path of suffering, overcoming it, and seeking the completed Adam, who symbolizes the conclusion of re-creation?

When we think of this, we should reflect on the historical background of God taking responsibility for the process of restoring that one person. How many twists and turns must there have been? Individuals must have witnessed their own misery, families must have seen it, nations must have experienced it, and countries must have seen it too. If it is tedious, it is a tedious period; if it is miserable, it is a miserable period; if it is unjust, it is unjust... If God were to think of Himself in such a position, it would undoubtedly be an historically tedious period that He could not give up. However, while overcoming that, God must have had many scenes of internal struggle, looking forward to a future time.

When we think of this, it is undeniable that God, as the Creator of heaven and earth, who could dominate everything under His authority, has endured the hardships of the salvation providence. If God were to think of His own dignity and abilities, and if He were to assert, "I am this kind of being," could He have maintained the path of seeking to find one human being in the historical process? I believe He could not have. If He were to assert Himself, think of Himself, and place Himself in a position of dignity, could He have endured the path of suffering to find a fallen human being? 

Knowing God's heart, Jesus willingly walked the path of the cross
When we think of this, if God Himself has a thought of self-interest, then there is nothing that can be done. However, if God is in a position of forgetting Himself, He could not continue this path. When we consider this, if God has gone through such a process, for whom has He done it? It was not for Himself. For whom is He enduring this? It is not for His own sake but for humanity. Who are these humans? It is for every individual. While there are billions of people today, it is not for the entirety of humanity but to pave the way for each individual.

When we see it this way, we must recognize that this is the truth. If there is someone who holds onto us and cannot let us go, who cannot abandon us on the path of suffering, how grateful we should be for that person. What could we use to express our gratitude? There may not be anyone like that in the world, but if there were, how could we repay that gratitude?

Then, until Jesus came to this earth, the effort of God must have been immense. How great must that effort have been? Finally, when the Messiah was sent to this earth, Jesus was presented as the representative of the fulfillment of God's wishes, having made decisions from God's heart and having gone through that effort. When Jesus was presented as the central being who could resolve the grievances of that effort, the nation should have accepted Him, and humanity should have hoped for unity. Yet, they opposed Him and drove Him to the point of death. If we think of this from God's perspective, how much resentment must He have felt after enduring thousands of years of suffering and overcoming it? How miserable must it have been for God to face the fate of having His Son killed? Yet, He did not vent His anger and had to silently extend the providence of salvation. How immense must have been the internal struggles of God? We humans do not think about this.

When Jesus was to be crucified, He said, "Abba, Father! If it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Yet, not my will, but yours be done." Those are the kinds of people who can move history and become the center of the times. Why must it be so? Because God exists, and God has a responsibility to protect such people, so those people become the center. Therefore, when you return today, think about it.

If you make a promise, you must keep it, even if it leads to ruin. I owe a debt to my parents. More so, I owe a debt to my mother. I have helped countless people, but I have not even been able to buy my mother a single piece of clothing. Yet I do not think of it as being in debt to my mother. Instead, I will do for all people what I could not do for my mother, and I will do it before God… Because of my mother’s debt, when all people are able to honor and God is able to honor, that mother will be able to receive blessings as a condition of the benefits she never received from her son. You must understand that.

God’s public justice does not change. No matter how murky the world becomes or how lost the direction of history may be, the laws of God’s justice flow without losing direction, even from deep within. You must understand that. It is simple. What will you leave behind? What will you leave as a debt? You need to know this…

A debt… When you face someone, isn’t it so? If you are grateful for even a word, you say, “Thank you,” right? That is all part of repaying debts. If you give someone a glass of water in summer, you say, “Thank you,” right? You honor them? That is all part of repaying debts. It’s all a game of repaying debts, all of it. Saying you won’t incur debt is just a game to avoid incurring debt. All manners and gifts are the same. Even if you set conditions, living by the law of remission to avoid incurring debt is the essence of life that you cannot deny.

Yes, until now, I have never prayed, “Oh! I need money, please give me money.” I find that trivial, so I have never prayed that way. I have prayed for people, but not for money… When you pray for people, money just comes. If there are people, money will come.

I have had three slogans until now. One is about faith… When I stand before God, I must believe what the world cannot believe! There is nothing I cannot believe when centered on God! If there is a command from God to even sacrifice my parents, I will practice that! How great must be the circumstances of God giving such commands that transcend human morality? If that can become a condition for the salvation of the world, then I must do it. Even if it leaves a name of unfilial conduct in history… But before God, isn’t that not unfilial? Give me the most unbelievable command, God! What did I pray for next? A faith like Peter’s, a faith greater than Peter’s…

What comes next? Wisdom! Without having a clear subjectivity in judgment, one cannot be a leader. Grant me wisdom greater than that of Solomon!

And what comes next? Love! I must love in a way that Jesus could not! Therefore, transcending nations, when I manifest love, there will be no one who does not look to me. Everyone will be drawn to me by that love. Since the end times are a period when love is dry, love is needed above all to initiate a new movement in that world.

These three things are what I have prayed for until now. As I prayed for them, I realized that they have all come to fruition. I have become someone who can perform acts that are always unbelievable. Do you understand what I mean? I am not someone who plays the game of believing. That’s why the people of the world already say, “Reverend Moon cannot be trusted.” I have become someone who cannot be trusted. That is not a bad meaning. I have become someone who can perform acts shrouded in strange mysteries.

I have also established principles on how to handle personnel matters as a person in charge. I have moved according to principles that no one can oppose. Regarding love as well… Americans and Germans regarding me… This time, an international revival group came from 25 countries, and when I entered the Haeundae Far East Hotel, all the hotel managers and staff were saying, “About 600 foreign people are coming, oh! Reverend Moon of the Unification Church has come.” They stood outside the glass windows and watched… Seeing that atmosphere, it felt like a dream.

They thought the Unification Church was here to train them, but they brought people who would become Reverend Moon’s arms and legs, willing to die if necessary. When did they all become like that? Even if you research it, you wouldn’t know. What did they create? They became that way themselves. Why? Because of God’s love. That’s why, when I give a command, I can receive reports on all the secrets of the parents in that household, and if I were a tyrant, I could wield all kinds of power. Why? Because those people love me.

If I say this to you, I don’t know. Do you love me? “Yes.” How much? How much do you love me? Why do you love me? Is it because food comes out? That’s how it is. When I see that, I know it is not for my own greed. When I pray, “Give me food, give me knowledge, give me power,” that is trivial. I do not pray that way. This is an important issue that must remain as the center of history in the eternal historical era. If you have faith, you must have loyalty. You must have loyalty. If you make a promise, you must keep it, even if it leads to ruin. “Oh! I made a promise, but I don’t want to fail.” That is… Heaven does not work that way. If you make a promise, you must gladly endure it.

In the same way, you must set your own goals. The fact that I have set such a goal means I must not incur debt. I must not incur debt before God, and I must not incur debt before God’s will, so I prayed for this important issue to resolve it.

Let’s strive not to incur debt. 

So, what is a good person? In terms of a university professor, it is a professor who teaches with a heart full of tears while receiving a meager salary. He will become an excellent professor. Why? Because he is not in a position to incur debt; he is in a position to repay debts. So, it is something that remains. This is how it is seen. When parents are struggling financially and cannot provide materially for their children, but with tears and love flowing from their bones and marrow, they prioritize their children above anyone else, that child is indebted to that mother more than anyone else. 

Children who understand this… In fact, filial piety does not come from wealthy families. You can see that many filial children come from poor families. Because the mother has passed down such a tradition, when the children inherit that tradition and strive not to incur debt to their mother, that mother feels the worth of having raised her child.

It is the same. For the Republic of Korea to prosper, its citizens must vow to be indebted to the Republic of Korea… There is no need for citizens who expect free products, donations, or anything else. If there are citizens who can say they will incur debt to their nation, that nation will prosper.

Then what will happen to the Unification Church? For the members of the Unification Church to dominate the world, even if they are in any department of the world, they must have the conviction that they will not incur debt, that they will repay debts. When that conviction can transcend any environment and scope in the world, the Unification Church will earn the respect of the world. It will become the center.

Why is that? Just as God has held the authority of being the center of the universe until now, even if it may not appear so, it will stand as a result of not losing its central position. This is the principle of human society, the core of God’s providence. Therefore, I have spoken to you in the hope that you will become those who do not incur debt and those who relieve debts.

Now, when I shout from one place, in the past, it was a sad time when I asked to be saved, but now we are entering a new awakening era where we can say, "Follow us," and I sincerely hope that each of us will not forget this time and be able to fulfill this mission with all our love.

We are no longer those who are always in the shade, but now we are advancing into a time when we can stand in the high mountain area before the bright heavens and earth and cry out to the world through the trumpet sound or through broadcasting. The third seven-year course must plan vast things that can be revealed on a flat surface and influence the world, and I know that I am in a position to do so, so I sincerely hope that you will be with me.

As I once again pledge my loyalty to the remaining purpose, we deeply repent and reflect on what we have lacked in the past, not only regretting but also this miserable self...

I earnestly ask and wish to become good ancestors, good pioneers, and good warriors of nation-building.

Today marks the beginning of April. In just a few hours, I will depart for Busan, so Father, please carry out Your plan. I do not wish to speak of my own desires. I have repented for the responsibilities I have failed to fulfill before You, placing my nation’s destiny in Your hands, and I have come to stand in a position where I must take responsibility for the future path of our nation.

Father! From now on, even if I dislike it, I cannot avoid the responsibility of a global struggle, and I know that even without money, I cannot refrain from economic involvement, realizing my own pitiful state. **A New Future for Humanity**
— Words from the Hopeful Day Grand Assembly in Busan —

I am the person just introduced, Moon Sun-myung. I sincerely thank all of you, ladies and gentlemen, for gathering here this evening. I apologize for the unexpected arrival of international youth from various places, causing disturbances in Busan, which was already troubled. I understand that you may have been curious about who this Moon person is, the one responsible for these disturbances. I stand before you today, and though I may not be handsome, I would appreciate your kind evaluation. (Applause) Thank you.

The title I wish to discuss with you today is "A New Future for Humanity." I will speak on this topic.

**The Reality of Humanity in Chaos and the Path of New Hope**

Among the countless people living on this earth, we know that no one has ever pursued true, eternal love, ideals, happiness, and peace. However, in this changing reality, amidst the increasing chaos, we are confronted with the fact that humanity is suffocating in a dead-end, struggling to find the ideal conditions it seeks.

We have come to a time where we must acknowledge that if there exists an eternal, absolute, unique, and unchanging being beyond this changing human world, it is only through that being that we can find these hopeful conditions. If such a being exists, it must be God. Therefore, we believe that only through discovering a new understanding of God, different from what we have known until now, can we bring new hope to this suffocating world.

If God exists, He cannot help but desire true love. He must also desire true ideals, true peace, and true happiness. God is undoubtedly the King of Love, the King of Ideals, and the King of Peace and Happiness. Thus, the conditions of love, ideals, happiness, and peace that He demands must be sought by humanity in a way that aligns with His expectations, as there is no other way for a true world of love, happiness, and ideals to manifest in our human world.

Even if God exists, concepts like love, ideals, happiness, and hope cannot be established by God alone. These concepts can only exist in a relative context, meaning that regardless of how absolute God may be, to achieve His love, ideals, peace, and happiness, there must be a relative existence before Him. (Applause) Thank you.

So, if we ask what can exist as a relative counterpart to God in this universe, everyone would answer that it is humanity. Since God cannot accomplish His love, ideals, peace, and happiness by Himself, it can only be achieved through a relative existence, which is humanity. We have not yet realized that without humanity, God cannot fulfill His love, ideals, peace, and happiness.

Today, we must recognize that this existence called "I" is absolutely necessary for the fulfillment of God's ideals and love. I believe we must restore the inherent value of humanity.

To all of you present here this evening, many may think that humans can just live and die without purpose, but that is not the case. In fulfilling the ideals of the absolute creator who created the heavens and the earth, if each of you understands that you are absolutely necessary, then a more hopeful path will open in your lives. (Applause) Thank you.

**Humans Desiring a Superior Existence**

I would like to ask you one thing: when you were young, did you wish to find a partner who was inferior to you or one who was superior? The answer would be the same for everyone: a superior partner. This conclusion would hold true regardless of cultural background. Furthermore, when loving parents regard their children, no parent wishes for their child to be inferior.

When a beautiful couple has their first child, regardless of how the child's appearance may differ from theirs, if they praise the child by saying, "Your child is so wonderful, perhaps even more so than you," the parents' joy would be immense. No parent would say, "Can you say that in comparison to the father and mother?" 

Then, who do humans resemble in this regard? We cannot claim that humanity is a causal existence. We exist as a result of certain causes. Results cannot occur without a cause. Regardless of the circumstances, the outcome must correspond to the cause. When we think about this, we must recognize that humanity must resemble some cause. 

If we ask who that causal existence is, we conclude that it is God, and thus humanity has become what it is by resembling God.

If we pose this question to God, asking, "God, you created this universe and are omnipotent, but if you desire a counterpart, do you want one who is superior or inferior to you?" we can anticipate that God would respond, "Why ask? I would certainly desire a being superior to myself."

Moreover, if we were to ask God whether He wishes for His own child to be inferior, He would have to respond, "No, I desire my child to be superior." Through this conclusion, we reflect on the fact that humanity, standing in the position of a child, should desire God to be of greater value and higher than ourselves, a thought we have never considered before.

**Humanity as God's Eternal, Unchanging, Absolute, Unique Counterpart**

Today, established theologians say, "The Creator and the created cannot stand on equal ground." If that is true, then through whom will love be realized, and through whom will ideals, happiness, and peace be achieved? There cannot be a relationship without a counterpart.

Is the love spoken of in Christianity meant to exist without people? Is the kingdom that will be established upon the Lord's return meant to exclude humanity? Absolutely not. It is love and ideals that must be realized through God and humanity. Therefore, we must recognize equal value in the existence of children. This is undoubtedly a logical conclusion.

From this perspective, we have not realized that our inherent value as humans is astonishing, dignified, and authoritative. If God exists, we must engage in a movement to restore this inherent value. Furthermore, humanity must also strive to find this value. We cannot deny the historical pursuit of morality and ethics in this regard.

Taking a step further, if God is eternal, unchanging, absolute, and unique, would He think, "Ah, I only need you when I need something from you"? No, He cannot think that way. Because He loves, because He is ideal, because He is the subject of happiness and peace, the relationship must be absolute, eternal, and unchanging. Therefore, His counterpart must also be an absolute, eternal, and unchanging existence. We must understand this fact.

Even in our fallen human world, lovers refer to each other as "my eternal counterpart, my unique and unchanging one." Humans do not wish for change... The more ideal God is, the less He can change. From this perspective, if humanity can stand within the realm of God's love and ideals, then if God is eternal, humanity must also be eternal. Even if humanity stands in the position of a counterpart, if God is absolute, humanity must possess absolute value as a counterpart. Likewise, if God is unchanging, humanity must also be an unchanging existence from the standpoint of a counterpart. From this perspective, the fact that humanity must be eternal is theoretical.

Among those present, there may be some who do not believe in religion. However, if among you here this evening, there are those who recognize that if such facts are true, and if there is an eternal God, then as children of God, humanity must also be eternal, those individuals will surely experience significant transformations in their lives, and a new flame of hope will ignite. 

**Where to Place the Origin of True Love, Happiness, Peace, and Ideals**

Now, I believe it has been established that God is the subject and humanity is the object. Therefore, what God must consider in this subject-object relationship is where to start the criteria for true love, happiness, peace, and ideals. The origin of these must be a matter of concern for God, who is the King of Wisdom.

In other words, there are two paths: one where the subject, God, says to the object, "You exist for me," and another where God, as the subject, gives to the object. 

What God must consider is where to establish the unchanging origin that can fulfill ideal conditions. If God stands in the position of "You must exist solely for me," then every being that stands in a subjective position, modeled after God, will emphasize "You must exist for yourself." In this case, a unified world cannot be established. However, if we establish the principle that "I exist for the other," and that the subject exists for the object, then we can finally become one and establish all conditions for development.

Therefore, when God considers where to place the origin of ideal conditions, He cannot place humanity in a position where they exist solely for Him, which is why He must establish the principle that He exists for humanity as well. I understand this to be God's position.

True love does not exist to be served. The standards of true ideals, true happiness, and true peace do not exist to be served. They begin with the desire to serve. Therefore, true spouses, true parents, true siblings, and true patriots do not begin with self-centeredness but with self-investment. The creator itself is the investment.

**The Principle Established by God: "Exist to Serve"**

When we look at this principle, what kind of parent is a true parent? A true parent is one who believes they were born for their child, lives for their child, and dies for their child. When they stand in the position of having existed, lived, and died for their child, they are undoubtedly a true parent, a loving parent, an ideal parent, presenting the conditions of peace and happiness to their child.

Then, what kind of child is a true filial son? A true son is one who believes they were born for their parents, lives for their parents, and dies for their parents. When they come to the position of being born for their parents, living for their parents, and dying for their parents, investing all their intellect and life into that position...
find a true filial child. When we look at that filial child, he is the son of love, the filial child of love, the son who embodies the ideals that parents desire, and the place where he is met becomes the source of peace. The parents who meet him can become happy parents. In the creation of the universe, it is undeniable that the principle of existence was established to serve the ideal origin that beings must possess. (Applause) Thank you.

What kind of husband is a true husband? It is the same. A husband who says, "I was born for you, I will live for you, and I will die for you," is a true husband. A true wife is the same. "I was born for you, I live for you, and I will die for you!" If a family can possess the principle of transcending oneself while corresponding to each other, that family can finally be an ideal family, a family of love, a happy family, and a family of peace.

The fact that God established such heavenly principles is something that humanity today does not know. If you, who have gathered here this evening, wish to have a heart that longs for a world of ideals, love, happiness, and peace, then by taking the path that can change your direction, that world can be a possible world before you.

Until now, we have thought, "I study to succeed, and I was born because of myself." But that is not the case. There may be famous individuals here in Busan. They might think, "I have laid this foundation through such efforts, and as a proud member of society, I have no reason to bow my head to anyone!" But that is not all there is.

What is the original motive for a man’s birth and survival? A man was not born for himself. Even from a physiological perspective, a man is created to aim at a woman, and through a woman, he can fulfill the conditions to become one. That is what a man is. In other words, he was born because of a woman. Saying this may please women and upset men, but in any case, we can conclude that a man was born because of a woman.

The same applies to women, who are the opposite of men. For whom was a woman born? "Oh, I am a woman. I put on makeup and beautify myself to feel good and live without envy of others... I was born for myself," one might think, but not at all! No matter how beautiful a woman is, everything she does to beautify herself is not for herself; it is for men. This fact cannot be denied.

Therefore, an ideal couple must recognize the original source from which each was born. Since a man cannot be born without a woman, a man must have a mindset of respect for women. Likewise, a woman must understand that a man has become the subjective motive for her existence and must have a heart that can elevate men fundamentally. With such a mindset, both men and women must step into a life of mutual support and a place where they can die for each other in order to become an ideal couple. Only then can they form an ideal couple.

Now you have discovered a formula here this evening. It is through the process of existing for others that one can fulfill an ideal. Therefore, no matter how great a person may be, they cannot pursue ideals and happiness outside of this formula. Just as humans cannot escape the fate of death, it is a fact that one can only find love, happiness, ideals, and peace by following the standards of the heavenly principles established by God. Now, if you center your judgments in your life journey around this official standard through such a perspective, you will discover that no one can fulfill the ideal conditions that humanity desires without going through this process.

Heaven is established in serving others. 

If we apply this formula to find a patriot of a nation, who is a patriot? A person who says, "I was born for my country! Everything I have lived for since I became aware has been for my country, and I will dedicate my life for my country," is undoubtedly a patriot. Therefore, it is reasonable to conclude that the Korean people praise General Yi Sun-sin as a patriot for this reason.

We can further develop this formula to discern who the greatest saints in human history are. Who is a saint of a higher dimension? It is determined by who has lived with a higher perspective for humanity. In this regard, I think that Jesus Christ is undoubtedly the greatest saint to have appeared in history.

Why do I say this? He was originally prepared for humanity and lived for 30 years for humanity, and even to the point of dying on the cross for humanity. At the moment he was crucified, he was in a position to curse the Roman soldiers who nailed him, yet he said, "Father, forgive them, for they do not know what they do," praying for them. This fact shows that he lived with a standard that could even serve his enemies, and because he died for humanity, I cannot help but conclude that he is the greatest of saints.

One thing we humans must understand is this: no matter how long we live on this earth, we will eventually pass away within a hundred years. In Korean, it is said that we return when we die. Where do we have to return? If God exists, who is the ancestor of humanity, the father of humanity, and in a subjective position regarding humanity, where do we have to go? We must return to where He is.

Today, whether in Christianity or Buddhism, when they speak of heaven or paradise, what kind of world is that homeland? I think many of you may not have a clear understanding of that world. However, I am someone who has been given the gift to have experiences of that world.

So what exactly is heaven? It is simple. What kind of structure is that place? In short, that world is the world for those who have existed for others. It is not a place for those who have lived for themselves. Only those who have lived for God and humanity can go there. I have come to realize this clearly.

No matter how devoted a church leader or believer may be, if that devotion is not for God and humanity, but rather ends up being self-serving, they will ultimately not enter heaven. They absolutely cannot enter. However, those who do not live for themselves but follow the principles of existence for others, living for God and humanity, even to the point of sacrificing their lives... those who walk the path of dying not for themselves but for God and humanity will undoubtedly find themselves in heaven.

We humans live like travelers. Just as your position can be morning, noon, evening, or night, young people are like the morning, youth is like noon, and those who have passed middle age are like evening. Those over 70 or 80 are like entering a dark night. Truly, we are in the position of travelers.

Humans do not realize their fallen state, but if God knows of humanity's fallen state, then He has the responsibility to lead fallen humans back to the path of their homeland. However, God does not lead humanity blindly. Through the historical process, He must guide them through the training process of religion, teaching them step by step how to live for God, through individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world. That is why religions have been established.

So why does religion say to be meek and humble, to sacrifice and serve? What is the reason for this? Why must we do so to enter heaven? Why must we do so to reach that land? It is because the homeland is organized in such a way. Therefore, in order to harmonize with that place, training is necessary here. Thus, the higher the religion, the more it emphasizes self-denial and the principle of sacrificial service.

The fact that religion has emphasized sacrificial service throughout historical eras is to leave the laws of that homeland on this earth. Therefore, the existence of such religions in the historical process cannot deny that God has been providentially guiding history. We inevitably reach the conclusion that God exists through history.

Thus, one cannot enter heaven without religion. What is the highest teaching that religion teaches? It is to absolutely live for God and absolutely live for humanity. There is nothing else. Even if the Bible consists of 66 books, all 66 books conclude with these two statements: "Live for others." The purpose of the Old and New Testaments is to establish this meaning, and many scriptures conclude with these two statements.

The Bible tells us, "Whoever wants to be exalted must be humbled, and whoever wants to be humbled will be exalted." Where is such a paradoxical logic? If I tell young people this, they might feel uncomfortable just thinking about it. However, this is the truth, and this content can fundamentally form the foundation of Christian life, as it aligns with the principles of that homeland and is a relative relationship. Therefore, those who walk this path will undoubtedly go to heaven.

That is why the Bible says, "There is no greater love than to lay down one's life for a friend." Why is there no greater love than this? What is the basis for this? This indicates that the existence of heaven and earth began with those who lived for others. When we consider this content, it is not a paradoxical statement. It is a principled statement. Then why does this principled statement conflict here? Because it has been corrupted by opposing results. When viewed this way, it is a valid logic. Here, you have learned the necessity of religion.

Reasons why God established the principle of existing for others. 

Why must God establish this principle of existing for others? I will mention a few reasons. Why could God not help but establish the principle of existing for others? Look, I want to ask you one thing. If someone truly dedicates themselves and sacrifices everything for you, when it comes to repaying that grace, is your true intention to take 50 percent of the 100 percent grace received and pocket it, while only repaying the remaining 50 percent? Or is your true intention to repay 100 percent or more? Which one is it? Even in a fallen world, when we probe our true intentions, we all conclude that our true intention is to repay 100 percent or more. It is because of that heart that salvation is possible, and it is because of that heart that we have the potential to align with the eternal world.

Let’s say person A has given person B 100 percent grace. When B repays that grace, they do not wish to repay less than 100 percent. They have a desire to repay more. So let’s say they repay 110 percent. When A thinks about the sincerity behind B’s repayment of 110 percent, A will feel grateful and want to give more. As this giving and receiving continues, it naturally increases. What does this mean? When a moving object makes one complete turn, it loses energy, but in this case, the more we give and receive, the more it increases. Therefore, the concept of eternity is established here. That is why God, the King of Wisdom, cannot help but establish the principle of existing for others. Only here can there be eternity. Outside of this, we cannot find the concept of eternity.

Since God also exists for others, He seeks out an object with which He can eternally give and receive. Therefore, if the standard for eternal giving and receiving is established, God's will is fulfilled. Moreover, if giving and receiving is eternal, it will continue to grow, leading to prosperity and development.

What is happiness? Isn’t it that we must improve to be happy? That is the ideal. Is it ideal to decline and diminish? No. Because God knows this truth, He cannot help but establish the principle of existing for others. Those who exist for others can be eternal, and because there can be development and prosperity in existing for others, we must understand that God could not help but establish such heavenly principles.

Next, what is the second reason? Look, let’s say there are eight family members in a household. If the youngest sibling dedicates themselves wholeheartedly day and night for the sake of the eight family members, what happens to that sibling over time? Rather than being pushed out, they are embraced more and more. As time passes, their father and mother, as well as their siblings, will come to value that youngest child more. No matter how small the child or younger sibling may be, they will become a central figure in the family. This is the heavenly principle.

Why must it be this way? Just as God exists for others and is the center of the universe, those in a position of being an object must also advance to a central position of existing for others in order to stand before the absolute center. Therefore, those who stand in such a position will undoubtedly become central figures. Isn’t that so?

What kind of person should the county chief, who is the central figure of the county, be? The county chief must...
You must be a person who exists for others. You must be a person who exists for the military more than anyone else. Also, what kind of person should a governor, representing the province, be? (Applause) Thank you. That governor must be a person who exists for the province more than anyone else. We must elect such a person. Furthermore, what kind of person should the president of the country be? Through the past, present, and future, they must exist for the country more than anyone else. If such a ruler exists, they cannot help but be a historical sovereign.

Today, when we tell our young people to live for others, they dislike it. "Why should I live for others during this short life? How long do people live? Why should I live for others during my brief youth?" But this is because they do not understand this principle. If they realize that this principle is indeed correct, young people will eagerly follow the path of living for others.

To you parents, when you educate your children and say, "Hey, do good things for others," and they respond, "What good does that do?" how will you answer? Will you say, "Doing good is just good"? That won't work. It doesn't work. You must analyze the cause and explain, "This is why you should do this."

The same goes for religion. When told to do good deeds, they might ask, "What is doing good? What is goodness?" "Is just doing it considered good?" No. You must explain that you should do good deeds for these reasons, and that goodness is about serving others, not taking from them. It is about investing oneself.

Therefore, those who serve others will undoubtedly become central beings. Even if a historical figure faces rebellion and is exiled, or suffers oppression and becomes imprisoned, they will surely emerge as a central being. If they cannot become such a being on earth, they will undoubtedly do so after death. Those who do not welcome them as central beings will have to submit to them a thousand or ten thousand times, even in the spirit world. When you understand this principle, a strong power will arise from here, allowing you to navigate through any adversity in life in a rational way.

Everyone present here tonight, you all want to become great, right? You say, "I want to be the center of the Republic of Korea. I want to be the center of the world." And you can all achieve that. How can you do it? By saying, "I exist for humanity more than anyone else in history. I will live for humanity and die for humanity. I can endure any adversity and can even accept the path of dying for humanity." When the quantity, height, depth, and breadth of this commitment increase, you will become a global figure.

Until now, you did not know that those who exist for others become central beings. Not only that, but you did not realize that there is nothing greater than being under the influence of those who exist for others. You might think, "Where is such a saying? There is nothing more unjust and frustrating than being ruled by someone after being born as a man." But that is not true.

If you can be eternally influenced by someone who can truly serve you, that is happiness. It is happiness. Being under influence means stepping into a position where you can influence others, right? Is a son who is under the influence of his father an unhappy son? No. After being completely under influence, there is a principle of complete influence. That is the principle of give and take.

Therefore, when a father is approached by a dutiful son who says, "Father, I want this, do you like it?" the father is bound to respond positively. In the human world, it is because we have not encountered a true subject who can genuinely serve us that we feel this way. If there is a true subject who can serve us, we must recognize how happy it is to be under their influence.

If you were to visit the spirit world, you would realize that God is the central being of the universe. Therefore, everyone desires to draw closer to Him. Being under His influence and getting closer to Him is a wish that lasts for a thousand or ten thousand years, and that position is one you can be grateful for for a thousand or ten thousand years. When you realize that such a position exists, it is only possible within the world of principles that can serve others.

Thus, what is the biggest problem in today's political philosophy? There is no way to resolve the relationship between the ruler and the ruled. No one wants this. However, if we follow the principle of existing for others, we can solve this problem and make complete unity possible, a fact we have not yet realized. (Applause)

One more thing: "Then why couldn't God establish the principle of existing for others?" God would have to say, "Hey, hey, the love you pursue is not your love. The ideal you seek is not your ideal. Love is a shared possession, and ideals arise from a shared foundation." What kind of foundation is that? It is not a foundation that tells you to serve yourself. It is a foundation for serving others.

Therefore, where do the love and ideals that are more precious than life come from? They do not come from men. Can love exist alone? Can ideals exist alone? Try to think about it. Where does love come from? You might say, "It comes from me." But no matter how famous you are in the world, if you say, "Haha, I have love even when I am alone. Haha, I have ideals even when I am alone," you are a crazy person.

Where does love come from? It comes through the other. We have not theoretically organized that love cannot appear without the other. Ideals do not come from me; they come through the other. Thus, because love and ideals, which are more precious than life, are relative existences that come from the other, we cannot help but regard humanity as a noble existence. Therefore, we must establish a humble position of serving others. (Applause)

This is a grateful message. We did not realize that God, the source of the universe, was like this. We did not realize that God realized the ideals of the universe according to such principles of existence.

The ideal formula for humanity
Why is heaven a good place? Because there is an eternal subject and an eternal object that cannot be separated and cannot be let go of, heaven is a good place.
