Therefore, if we speak of the ideal formula, what is it? The husband must live for the wife, the parents must live for the children, and the family must live for the neighbors and relatives. How wonderful is that!

God's things are mine... To make God's things mine, I must rise to the highest position in the world, becoming a son or daughter whom God can recognize. Only then can I make God's things mine. If I say, "Oh, I am a child, and I am going to give up everything, oh, let’s just live for our family, oh, you and I are brothers, let’s just live for our parents," that is... digging a tunnel and building a fence to practice a path of suffering. You will now understand these things. Therefore, the true path of faith is truly difficult. The true means it should not change. Spring, summer, autumn, and winter do not exceed their limits, which is why summer can come. When spring is full, summer comes. Summer does not come arbitrarily. When summer reaches its limit, autumn comes. That is why autumn comes. If you let it go arbitrarily, autumn will not come. Autumn comes because it reaches its limit, and winter comes because autumn reaches its limit. Spring comes because winter reaches its limit. Therefore, the seasons that do not change become spring, summer, autumn, and winter, which is why they can be called true seasons. Isn’t that right? The same goes for you. The true does not change.

When you first entered the Unification Church, whether it was day or night, you were all running around as if living for a purpose, but after about ten years, you think, "Oh, I’ve seen it all! I’ve seen it all. It’s nothing special. Just have children, and after all this, it’s the church." That’s what you should see. (laughter) See how much of a mess that becomes….

You know that, and you will know it well. The true path of faith is truly difficult. It is a path that cannot be done freely. Everything must be aligned. Hoping that you will leave such a path in your life, I will conclude my words. 

<Prayer> Loving Father, we have come to understand the unfortunate fact that You have become powerless because there is a path of restoration that no one knows. We know that because You have drawn a chaotic historical process that no one can find, You have produced results that make You appear indifferent and bewildered. When we come to know that there has been such a difficult path of indemnity and restoration, history has become certain, and we have realized how certain this era has become.

**New Hope for Humanity**
— Words from the Hope Day Grand Festival Daegu Assembly —
I sincerely thank you, ladies and gentlemen, for gathering here today. I also apologize to the many guests outside this venue. I know that you have made great efforts to listen to my words despite difficult circumstances. I sincerely hope that you will participate with a joyful heart.

As you all know, the person standing here is none other than Moon Sun-myung. (Applause and cheers) I understand that I have been a subject of much controversy and that many of you have been quite curious about me. I may not be someone remarkable, but I sincerely hope that you will see me clearly and evaluate me well today. (Applause) I apologize for my hoarse voice.

Today, I would like to share my thoughts with you on "A New Hope for Humanity" and "A New Future for Humanity."

**Conditions for a New Future for Humanity**
To achieve a new future, we already know that what humanity has pursued and desired until now is not sufficient. For a new future to be realized, a new person must emerge. This new person will not simply arise from the ever-changing humans who cannot surpass their limits today, but rather, there must be an absolute and unchanging being through whom the new person can emerge.

So, who is that being? We cannot help but say that it is God. By knowing God from a new perspective, a new person can finally appear. Thus, we believe that a new future can be formed.

Throughout history, humanity has never ceased to pursue eternal and unchanging true love, ideals, happiness, and peace. However, as you all know, in this era of conflict and change, we have lost the possibility of finding the ideal conditions for love, happiness, and peace that humanity has pursued. Moreover, we are now facing a dead end, suffocating against a wall.

Despite all efforts, humanity finds itself in a miserable reality where it has lost even the possibility of fulfilling the true love, true ideals, true happiness, and true peace that it truly desires. 

Here, we recognize that if there is an eternal, unchanging, and absolute being beyond the changing human condition, that being cannot be anyone other than the God we know. If God exists, then God must be the center of true hope, true happiness, true peace, and true love that humanity desires. God is the king of love, the king of ideals, happiness, and peace. 

In order for God and humanity to enter a place where they share the same standard of hope and the same aspirations, we must clearly understand where true love begins and where true ideals, true happiness, and true peace originate. Without this understanding, we cannot fulfill the ideal conditions that humanity desires.

**God's Love, Ideals, Happiness, and Peace are Possible Through Human Beings**
If God exists, can God fulfill love alone? No, God cannot do that alone. Can God fulfill ideals alone? Can God enjoy happiness and peace alone? No, God cannot do that either.

As you know, love is not something achieved alone. Ideals, happiness, and peace are not realized in isolation but in relational contexts. Therefore, to fulfill God's ideals, there must be a counterpart. To complete God's love, there must also be a counterpart. Without a counterpart, God's happiness and peace cannot be realized. What can God do with love, ideals, happiness, and peace if God is alone? It can only be possible by establishing a counterpart.

From this perspective, if we ask who in this universe can be God's counterpart, we know well that there is no other being capable of being God's object other than human beings.

Today, we may think of ourselves as insignificant beings, but we must realize that without each individual, God's love cannot be completed, God's ideals cannot be fulfilled, and God's happiness and peace cannot be achieved. We must recognize that we are beings of higher value capable of completing God's love, ideals, happiness, and peace.

I want to ask you one thing. Many of you here are middle-aged or older. When you were young and looking for a partner, did you want someone less capable than yourself or someone more capable? I believe you would all give a common answer: it is natural to want a partner who is better than oneself, regardless of gender or age. Furthermore, I believe many loving parents are present here. No parent wishes for their beloved children to be less capable than themselves.

For example, if a handsome couple has a child who may not look like them, if someone praises that child by saying, "Your son or daughter is more wonderful than you," the parents' faces would light up with joy. This shows that it is a natural desire for parents to wish for their beloved children to surpass them.

**God's Desire for Eternal, Unchanging, Absolute, and Unique Counterparts**
When we consider this fact, we must ask, "Whom do humans resemble today?" Humans are undoubtedly not causal beings but rather result-oriented beings. Humans are born from some cause. Therefore, as result-oriented beings, they cannot be connected in a position that is contrary to their cause. The most theoretical outcome is one that resonates with the cause.

So, who do humans resemble when they desire a counterpart who is better than themselves, and when they wish for their beloved children to be better than themselves? It is because the causal God desires that, and as a result, humans, who are born as result-oriented beings, cannot help but demand the same.

If we ask God, "What about you? Do you wish for your object to be better than you?" how do you think God would respond? There cannot be a God who says, "I am God, so I wish for my object to be less capable." Furthermore, if God is in the position of a parent to humanity, when we ask, "Do you wish for your children to be less capable than you?" God cannot answer, "I wish for them to be less capable." God, too, must wish for the object to be better than Himself, and God must wish for His children to do better than Himself. This conclusion is inevitable, just as we humans cannot help but demand the same. (Applause)

You, who have gathered here today, have until now thought of yourselves as worthless beings. You have regarded yourselves as beings without value. However, upon reflection, we realize that when God wishes to elevate an object to His level, He desires that object to be more excellent than Himself. When He wishes to elevate His children, He desires them to be better than Himself. This is God's demand. Therefore, humanity, which has lost its inherent value, must seek to reclaim its noble and dignified human authority.

Even if there is a person who seems worthless, they possess characteristics that no one can infringe upon. Whether they are capable or not, they are God's sons and daughters. Centered on God's love, they can possess equal value and must restore their inherent human value. This is the inevitable mission of humanity. Even if you forget everything I have said today, please remember that God wishes for us to become such noble beings.

Until now, modern theology has concluded that the Creator and the created cannot stand on equal ground. If that is the case, what can God do with love? What can God do with ideals? What can God do with happiness? Without humanity, God's love is unnecessary. God's ideals are unnecessary. God's happiness and peace are unnecessary. We must understand that these things only become necessary in the presence of humanity.

God is eternal, absolute, unique, and unchanging. Therefore, when we stand in the position of such an object, do we wish to change? No, we do not. We desire to possess the value of a unique, unchanging, and absolute object.

In today's fallen human world, even the fallen human desires that their beloved remain eternal. They wish for their beloved to be the only one. They do not want their beloved to change. Even fallen humans demand the eternal, unchanging, absolute, and unique nature of their beloved. Would the God who is the center of the universe wish for His object of love to change? No, that cannot be. Would He wish for the existence of His object to be limited? No, He desires it to be absolute. We must understand that He wishes for the existence of His object to be unchanging.

From this perspective, if we clearly understand that today, our lives are God's objects and that we are His sons and daughters who can receive His love, then we must recognize that the concept of eternal life is a highly theoretical conclusion.

**The Origin of True Love, Ideals, Happiness, Peace, and the Origin of the Fall**
I wonder if there are any among you here who do not believe in religion, but when you discover that you stand in the position of a human being who can regard God as the subject and Father, you must understand that being able to be the object of His love, ideals, peace, and happiness means that you will attain eternal life. If you think that those living on this earth will simply live for 70 or 80 years and then pass away, that is a misunderstanding. Because God is eternal, humanity must stand in the position of His eternal object and children, which is why humanity must attain eternal life. We must understand that we are meant to attain eternal life.

Now you have understood the subject-object relationship where God is the subject and humanity is the object. Now, what is the next issue that arises? There is something that the wise King God cannot overlook, which is the question of where to place the origin of true love, true ideals, true happiness, and true peace.

Now the issue is that we must clearly understand the origin of true love. Without realizing the origins of true ideals, true happiness, and true peace, we cannot participate in and achieve God's eternal love, ideals, happiness, and peace. Therefore, the wise King God must consider where to place the origin of all these things.

When viewed from the perspective of the subject, there are two directions: one where the object serves the subject and another where the subject serves the object.

If the principle is established that the object must serve the subject, and if anyone standing in the position of the subject adopts that stance, then this world cannot form a unified world. It will lead to division.

Therefore, when the wise King God considers where to place the origin of happiness, He must place the origin of true love, true happiness, true ideals, and true peace in a way that allows the subject, God Himself, to exist for the object. 

**The Principle of Creation is to Exist for Others**
What is the fall of humanity? The fall of humanity is the result of centering on oneself and seeking to exist for oneself. Adam and Eve were meant to exist for God in the Garden of Eden, yet they stood in a position where they sought to have everything serve themselves, despite God existing for humanity. This is the origin of the fall. Here, humanity and history have been turned upside down.

A person who is self-centered is proud when viewed individually. When we look at the leaders of a nation, if they stand in a position where the entire nation exists for themselves, or if they stand in a position where the whole world exists for them, those who advocate such a stance will be concluded to be dictators. Thus, we must understand that the wise King God established the principle of "exist for others" at the time of creation. (Applause)
There have been many men who have come here, and the question is, why were men born at all? If you ask, "Why were men born?"... you have lived up until now with the thought that "a man is a man, born for himself. If I am from Daegu, I live proudly with authority, not envying anyone, and I was born for myself and live for myself." However, when you examine the essence, it is not so.

The reason men were born is not because of men themselves. Men were born because there is a counterpart, women. Men were born to represent women. Essentially, men were born for women. Women were not born for themselves either. Women were born for men. They were born with the position to care for each other.

You may have taken a bus or something to come to this gathering today. Men have broad shoulders, and women have wider hips, so when they sit together in a bus seat, it fits perfectly. This indicates that they are in a position to complement and support each other. No matter how accomplished a man is, he was not born for himself. He was born for women. No matter how beautiful a woman is, she was not born for herself. She was born for men. We cannot ignore the fact that the origin of existence began with the purpose of caring for others.

From this perspective, we can find a fundamental principle of how God created the ideal world. True love can only start from existing for others, the ideal partner can only manifest from existing for others, peace can only be achieved from existing for others, and happiness can only be realized from existing for others. I hope you remember this today.

For example, what kind of person is a true parent? What exactly is a true parent? There is no separate category for true parents. They were born for their children, they live for their children, and they can die for their children. A parent who stands in a position to dedicate everything for their children is a parent of true love, true ideals, true happiness, and true peace. We must understand that only in existing for others can eternal, unchanging love, ideals, happiness, and peace be established.

Where can we find true couples? Where can we find couples with true love and ideals? The conclusion is the same. A husband is born for his wife, lives for his wife, and dies for his wife. A wife is born for her husband. She lives for her husband and dies for her husband. It is not about living for oneself.

If such couples appear, they can receive God's love, become the object of God's peace, and become the substantial embodiment of God's ideals. They are undoubtedly true and eternal ideal couples, couples of love, partners of peace, and happiness.

Patriots, saints, God, and heaven are all achieved through existing for others. We must understand that God, being the king of wisdom, established such principles of creation. True love can only emerge from existing for others, and true ideals, true happiness, and true peace can only be established in this way. I hope you can understand this.

Then, what kind of person is a true patriot? The same applies here. A person is born for their country, lives for their country, and does not live for themselves. They live for their country. They die for their country. Such a person cannot help but be a patriot. If we were to select such a person, they would undoubtedly be someone like Admiral Yi Sun-sin.

Expanding the scope further, we can also find who the true saints in human history are by applying this principle. When we look through this principle, Jesus Christ must be the greatest among saints. Some of you may not be Christians, but let me explain why.

Just before he was crucified, despite being surrounded by Roman soldiers and all those who opposed him, Jesus did not curse or mock them like an ordinary person would. Instead, he prayed for his enemies until the end. He was born for humanity, lived for humanity, and even as he died, he loved those who opposed him and prayed for them. There has never been anyone like him in history, and because he represents the essence of existing for others, it is reasonable to conclude that Jesus Christ is the greatest among saints.

From here, we must understand one thing through this principle: God is a being who exists for others. For six thousand long years, He has worked to save humanity, yet countless people have inflicted various kinds of abuse and persecution upon Him. However, He has come forth for humanity while enduring all of this. This fact cannot be denied.

Since God is such a central being, what kind of organization exists in the heaven where God resides? The structure is simple. Those who can go to heaven or paradise are not those who lived for themselves. Such people cannot go there. Heaven is the place where those who were born for the whole and lived for the whole go.

You may not have experienced the spiritual world, but I have experienced many spiritual realms through heavenly grace. When you enter that world, there is not a single person who lives for themselves. All those who lived for God and humanity are in that world.

Because God established these ideal principles and origins, the land of the original homeland must be a world created by that law. Therefore, for the countless people who seek to find that world, it is inevitable that such laws of the homeland must be taught on this earth.

If we summarize the entirety of the Old and New Testaments, it concludes with "exist for others." The stage for training to teach this law on earth is what we call religion. What is religion? It is to train individuals to adapt to the laws of their homeland when they return to their original home, to cultivate a character that can live according to those laws. This is the essence of religious life today.

The higher the religion, the less it emphasizes itself. The higher the religion, the more it emphasizes gentleness and humility. Furthermore, it emphasizes sacrificial service. Why must it be this way? Because that is the law of the homeland. Humans are, after all, like travelers seeking their homeland, so to train them to live according to the laws of their homeland, higher religions have taught the lesson of sacrifice.

When we look at the historical religions that have continued this mission, we cannot deny that God has governed through religion throughout history.

Today, whether you are religious or non-religious, whether you can enter the world of the homeland or go to heaven depends on whether you have lived more for others or for yourself throughout your life. Based on this, you will go to good places or bad places. You know this well. There is no need to ask. You know it well.

Therefore, even though you have lived for yourself until now, if you understand this principle and can now live for the Republic of Korea, humanity, and God, if your life becomes more about living for others than for yourself, it is inevitable that you will go to a good spiritual realm.

In countless religions, no matter how many scriptures there are, everything concludes with the two words "exist for others." If we summarize all 66 books of the Old and New Testaments, it all ends with "exist for others." Jesus said, "I did not come to be served, but to serve." He spoke with this thought in mind. Why? Because God established the principles of creation and the ideal standard to exist for others. Therefore, the son of heaven, who must represent the principles of the original world, must do so. That is why he emphasized that he came to serve. "Whoever wants to be exalted will be humbled, and whoever humbles themselves will be exalted." He said, "There is no greater love than to lay down one's life for one's friends." The conclusion is simply "exist for others." Here, heaven can manifest, and God can manifest. We can clearly infer through the scriptures that God's love, peace, happiness, and ideals can manifest.

No matter how much one has attended church, a person who does not know how to care for others cannot enter heaven. It is absolutely impossible. A true friend is one who knows how to care for their friends.

That is why everyone here today must exist for others. Only there can God, the center of principles, be found, and God operates through that foundation, determining His objects from that place. The sons and daughters of God are also determined from that place. We must understand that it cannot be established anywhere else. This is the problem.

Today, all humans say, "It must fit my heart." Everything must fit my heart. Husbands must fit my heart, in-laws must fit my heart, schools must fit my heart, and society must fit my heart. This way of thinking has taken root. We must turn this around. Without turning this around, we cannot manifest the world that God desires or the people that God desires on this earth. We cannot find the families that God desires, the tribes that God desires, the nations that God desires, or form humanity as God desires. Now, I believe you have understood this principle of existing for others.

The reason for establishing the principle of existing for others
Now, let us delve a step deeper. Why could God not help but establish the principle of existing for others? This is the question. Why must it be for others? This is what young people today dislike the most. "Oh, why should I live for others when I am so inadequate?" They think this is the most unpleasant thing to hear. Here, one issue arises: Why could God not help but establish the principle of existing for others? We must unravel this fundamental question.

So let me mention a few conditions. Let me ask you one thing. Is there anyone among you who has truly indebted their life to someone else 100 percent? When you want to repay that debt, do you want to put 50 percent in your pocket and repay only 50 percent, or do you want to repay 100 percent or more? Please answer. Everyone would say, "I want to repay 100 percent or more." This desire exists because we can return to the heavenly kingdom. Without this desire, salvation and everything else would be impossible. There is not a single person who wants to harm someone who truly cares for them. Because of this, those who truly care for others can all be saved.

God truly cares for humanity, and when humanity realizes that God cares for them 100 percent, they will repay all their debts to God. When that happens, all of humanity can be saved. This conclusion is established.

For example, if I have truly benefited person B 100 percent, and if he has received that benefit in a true sense, he will repay that benefit with 110 percent of his sincerity. If person A has given person B 100 percent, the return will increase to 110 percent. Do you understand? When we see that person B repays with 110 percent, person A wants to give 120 percent. That desire leads to person A repaying 120 percent. Thus, the more we give and receive, the more it increases, forming an eternal law of motion. This is where the concept of eternity is established. We must understand this. The concept of eternity is established here. Isn't that right? When you apply the same force in motion, it gradually diminishes, but because we apply more force, the motion continues eternally. Not only is eternal motion formed, but new developments also emerge from here. In other words, prosperity begins from there.

Because God knows these principles and laws... only in existing for others is there eternal life, and where there is eternal life, there is prosperity. Therefore, the wise king, God, could not help but establish the law to exist for others.

Next, let’s say there are eight family members in your household. Among those eight, if the youngest sibling is the one who cares for the family, who cares for the parents, and who is willing to dedicate everything, including their life, for the family, what kind of existence will that youngest sibling become if they continue to live like that? You must understand that such a sibling will inevitably emerge as the central being of that household. This is something we did not know today.

Moreover, the young people present here may think, "Caring for others is tiring." However, those who try to live for others become the central beings. When electing a leader who can represent the Republic of Korea today, the one who cares for the Republic of Korea more than anyone else becomes the central being. The principle that those who exist must be chosen as central beings is established here.

The God who created heaven and earth exists for the universe. Because He exists for others, He is the eternal central being. Because He exists eternally for others, He becomes the eternal central being.

Similarly, because humans are created in the image of God, a person who resembles God must be established as a central being. Therefore, it is inevitable that they become central beings; this is a fixed law. You must understand that.

Furthermore, the young men and women present here must care for the entire school if they are in school...
If you become that, you will become the exemplary student of that school. You will become a central being. This is a truth that needs no further explanation.  
Then what becomes possible? Up until today, the world has been divided into rulers and the ruled; this is the problem. There are those who rule and those who are ruled, and this has emerged as a difficult issue in politics until now. How will we resolve this? That is the question.  
When you stand in a position where you can truly care for others and a central being emerges, there is nothing beyond being subject to that central being. Today, you may see being subject to others as a shame, but if you are subject to someone who truly cares for you, there is no greater happiness than that. For example, when you go to the spirit world, there is no greater happiness than being subject to God, the eternal central being who exists for all creation. Once you are subject to that, you will want to be subject for a thousand years or ten thousand years. Similarly, we have not realized how happy it is to live under the guidance of someone who truly cares for you.  
Then what is the third point? Today, we humans have thought that love, ideals, and such are all ours. We have thought of them as our own. Anyone easily thinks that love is my love, happiness is my happiness, and if there are ideals, they are my ideals. But that is not the case. Love does not start from oneself. Ideals do not come from oneself.  
So where does love come from?  
Love comes from the object. Without an object, there is no love. Without an object, there are no ideals. Without an object, there can be no happiness or peace. This must come through the object. Because love and ideals, which are more precious than one's own life, come from the object, one must humbly prepare for that object to receive those precious things. Therefore, God cannot help but establish the principle of serving with a bowed head.  
In serving, there is eternity, in serving, there is prosperity, in serving, the center appears, in serving, the origin of peace and unity emerges, and in serving, true love and ideals are formed. This is why we must understand that God established the principle of existence for the sake of serving.  
What is the Unification Church?  
Now, everyone, what exactly is the Unification Church? This is the question. What does the Unification Church do? You may be curious about this. Even though the established churches have opposed it for nearly 30 years, saying things about Moon, the Unification Church remains silent and is said to be dead.  
If we look at it centered around God, the established churches are the older brothers. The Jewish church is the eldest brother, the Christian church is the second brother, and the Unification Church is the third. This is how I think about it. Just like the older brothers who tried to kill Joseph in the past, they say it out of spite. They ask for food, or they ask for a place to sit, or something else...  
However, not speaking does not mean they have no mouths, and not fighting does not mean they have no fists. When we see the law of a thousand miles, it is because they understand the principle of existing for the sake of others. Therefore, the Unification Church has followed this principle. Whether it is day or night, even if opposed, they say, "I don't know." God has forgiven those who oppose out of ignorance, so we cannot curse those who oppose the Unification Church out of ignorance.  
Today, if you look, young people from the West or young people from Japan are secretly approaching Korea. You may feel uncomfortable just hearing the word Japanese, right? I feel the same way. I am someone born of the Korean people, and I do not want to fall behind in patriotism more than anyone else.  
Why would those people follow Koreans if Koreans are not that great? Why would Westerners, who are struggling and not very good-looking, follow Koreans?  
However, what the Unification Church advocates is a solution that humanity must seek in this world of confusion and conflict, a solution that aligns with the principles of a thousand miles, human ethics, and social history. They follow this path because they know that if they do not go now, they will have to go in the future.  
So what do young people in the Unification Church educate about today? They know that the secret of creation is here, that love and ideals are here. If you want to meet God, if you want to have God's love, if you want to participate in God's peace and happiness, you must become a person who exists for the sake of others. There is nothing else. **New Future for Humanity**
— Words from the Hope Day Festival in Seoul —

I sincerely thank you, ladies and gentlemen, for gathering here this evening. I apologize for my hoarse voice.

The title of the message I would like to share with you today is "The New Future for Humanity." I will speak briefly on this topic.

The resolution of the various problems facing humanity in this chaotic situation begins with the establishment of a clear view of God. You all know well that the world we live in today is a chaotic one. After the Middle Ages, we have passed through an unclear era of theocentrism and have now arrived at an uncertain era of anthropocentrism. Moreover, we are in an era of materialism, which can be described as a materialistic age. All of this has resulted from the inability to present a clear content throughout the historical process while being in a state of confusion. Today, on April 14, 1975, we are facing a point of irretrievable de-ideologization.

Therefore, the issue for us now is not the lack of people or the lack of material. The problem arises from the absence of a clear view of God. If a clear view of God is established, then a new view of life and a new view of history through that view of God must be established; otherwise, a new future for the world cannot emerge. So what is the problem here? If we truly know God, then we believe that all the issues stemming from the unclear view of God that began to decline in the Middle Ages, the currents of anthropocentrism in the present age, and the issues of materialism will be resolved.

Therefore, the question of whether God exists or not cannot be avoided. I cannot help but think about how to leave an unforgettable impression on all of you gathered here this evening. So, where should we start thinking about God?

**Proving God's Existence Through the Human Body**

If we quietly observe ourselves, the most important part is the face. Among the face, the most important part is our eyes. If we think about this centered on our eyes and trace the history of these eyes, we can say they came from our parents. Then, where did the eyes of those parents come from? If we trace back through our ancestors to the first humans, we find that the fundamental history of the eyes rests there.

When the eyes were born, did they know that there was a sun in the sky? If we ask this, we must say that the eyes themselves could not know that there was a sun. Moreover, why do our eyes blink? It is because we know that moisture evaporates due to the sun and radiant heat on this earth. Furthermore, we have eyelashes, and we know that these eyelashes exist because there is dust in the air.

So, did the original eyes know that there was a sun in the sky? No matter how much we think about it, we cannot answer yes. Did the eyes themselves know that this earth has the ability for moisture to evaporate due to radiant heat? If we ask that, we cannot answer yes. Did the eyelashes know that there is air? If we ask whether the eyelashes knew that there was dust in the air to prevent it from entering the eyes, no one can answer yes.

When we look at our eyes, which are made of material, we cannot deny that their existence is based on astronomical knowledge. There was a sun before the eyes were created, there was air before the eyes were created, and there was evaporation before the eyes were created. The eyes themselves did not know this, but we cannot deny that someone knew this.

In other words, when we think about the fact that the eyes themselves arose based on biological knowledge, we must acknowledge that before the eyes existed, there was a sun, there was dust in the air, and there was moisture evaporating on this earth. Someone must have known this before humanity was born. In that state, the eyes were created to be able to adapt.

Even when we look at just our eyes, there are thousands of eye doctors. However, even eye doctors do not fully understand the mysterious and unknown world of the eyes. When we think about the fact that the eyes are a palace of infinite mysteries, we come to realize that there was an existence that knew all of this before the eyes were born and that it was inevitable for us humans to be born in this way.

When we realize that there is an origin that thought of something before any material or existence, we must acknowledge that this thinking subject is God. When we are born, we already know that we will be able to walk. This can be understood by looking at our eyebrows. Eyebrows were created to prevent sweat from flowing down from the forehead into the eyes.

Furthermore, your noses are similar. Why do your noses widen as they go down, and why do they have grooves on either side? It is to prevent sweat from flowing into the mouth. We cannot deny that this is a fact that was known in advance.

In this way, someone knew everything and allowed us humans to be born. So who is this knowing being? We cannot help but say it is God. In this sense, we must conclude that God exists.

**God's True Love, Ideals, Happiness, and Peace Are Possible Through Human Beings**

We humans have never ceased to long for true, eternal, and unchanging love, ideals, happiness, and peace. Such ideal conditions cannot be fulfilled through changing human beings. This is clearly evidenced when we look at the current world situation we are in today.

In such times, if there is an unchanging, absolute, eternal, unique, and immutable God, then we cannot help but demand the origin of true love, true ideals, true peace, and true happiness from that God. From that perspective, we can only welcome a new world of peace and happiness when we establish a view of God that sees God himself, a view of life that sees God himself, and a view of material that sees God himself.

What is the issue here? No matter how absolute God is, can that God achieve love, ideals, happiness, and peace alone? It is impossible for God alone. Love, ideals, peace, and happiness cannot exist in isolation. They are formed under relative conditions. Therefore, even if God is absolute, when there is no counterpart before God, the absolute love, absolute ideals, or absolute happiness and peace that God desires cannot be fulfilled.

From this perspective, what exists in this created world that can appear as an objective being before the absolute God? There is no other being besides human beings. Only humans possess the value to fulfill God's ideals, to complete God's true love, and to realize God's happiness and peace.

Thus, God is the subject, and we humans are the object. When we look at ourselves as the object before God, who can be the king of true love, the king of true ideals, and the king of true peace, we must recognize that we are beings of infinite value.

**Humans Want Their Objects to Be Better Than Themselves**

In the relationship between subject and object, I would like to ask you one thing: When a young man chooses a partner, does he want to choose someone inferior to himself or someone superior? If we ask this, the natural conclusion is that everyone wants to choose someone better than themselves. Furthermore, what parent wishes for their beloved child to be born inferior? No parent wishes for that; they desire a child who is better and more excellent than themselves.

Let’s say a handsome man or beautiful woman gets married and has their first child. When comparing the child's face to the parents' faces, it may not look like either parent, but when someone says, "Your child is even better looking than you," we see the parents beaming with joy. (Applause) This demonstrates that wanting one's partner or child to be better is a natural desire of human nature.

So, who do humans resemble when they have such demands? When we think about it, we cannot deny that humans are not causal beings but rather result-oriented beings. Causes must manifest through a certain content as results. If we humans wish for our objects or our children to be better than ourselves, it is only natural to conclude that this demand arises because we resemble the causal being, God. (Applause)

From this perspective, if we turn our question to God, asking, "God, do you also wish for your objects to be better than you? Do you wish for your son to be better than you?" we would find that God would also conclude, "I cannot help but give the same answer as you." (Applause)

Today, humanity thinks very poorly of its own value. Many people treat themselves as worthless, like animals. that you must understand that it cannot be anything other than our desire.

The Ideal Origin of Creation and the Origin of the Fall
Until now, we have not even considered the question of where to set the ideal origin of creation. What does the word creation itself mean? It refers to the input of everything. In order for thought itself to come into being, it must invest its own corresponding power. Existence begins from that investment.
When God thinks about the relationship between subject and object, there are only two paths. We must set the ideal origin of God here.
If all objective beings before the subject, God, are to absolutely obey and serve only the subject, what will happen? Just as God exists as a masculine subject, if among humans, the man is the subject and the woman is the object, then if the man also says to the woman, "Serve the subject," what will happen? The path to oneness will be blocked.
However, when the wise King, God, establishes a position where the object can say, "Serve," everything can become one. Therefore, where do we set the ideal origin of creation? In conclusion, we must understand that we cannot place it in a position that says to serve oneself, nor can we place it in a position that says to serve the other.

**Proving God's Existence Through the Human Body**

Let me take a moment to speak. When you look at a human face, it represents that person's character. By looking at a face, we can infer what that person's heart and nature are like. This face signifies that character.

So, whose likeness does the human face, which represents character, bear? If God exists, we must say it resembles God. As you know, when animals are born or when chicks break out of their eggs, the eyes develop first.

What does this eye symbolize? It can be said to symbolize God. What does the nose symbolize? It can be said to symbolize humanity. And what does the mouth symbolize? It can be said to symbolize all things. This very small face symbolically shows heaven, humanity, and earth.

Now, because the question of whether the spirit or matter came first is at stake, let us ask. Every morning when you wash your face, you look in the mirror. When you look, you see your entire face, but what is the focus? It is the eyes. 

When we inquire about the eyes, "Oh, eyes! Where did you come from?" they would respond, "Where did I come from? I came from my parents." If we trace the history of the eyes back to the ancestors of our ancestors, it leads us to the very first ancestors of humanity.

When the very first ancestor of humanity was born, did the eye itself know that "Ah, there is a sun in the sky"? No, it did not. The eye itself could not possibly know that there is a sun in the universe.

Furthermore, we see our eyes blinking. Why do they blink? It is not because they want to. The eyes blink to prevent moisture from evaporating due to the heat radiating from the sun. So, you know that the eyes blink for this reason.

Now, could the eye itself have thought, "Ah, when I come out into this world, moisture will evaporate, so I must blink to keep my eyes moist"? The material eye itself cannot think.

Moreover, we have eyelashes. Why do we have eyelashes? It is obvious. They prevent dust from entering the eyes because there is dust in the air. We understand that eyelashes serve this function.

So, when we ask whether our ultimate ancestor's eye could have known, "When I am born into the world, there will be dust in the air, so my eyelashes must be like this," what do you think? Do you think it knew? The eye itself could not have known that.

This is based on astronomical knowledge, knowledge of the solar system, knowledge of the spatial world, and all the knowledge about the inner and outer aspects of this earth. Given this fact, we cannot think that the eye itself knew and wanted to be that way. This fact cannot be denied.

In this light, the question arises: Is the eye itself first, or is thought first? When we ask whether the earth has a sun that causes moisture to evaporate and dust to be present, if one does not know and is simply that way, then that person can only be considered ignorant.

From this perspective, when we consider whether matter or thought came first, the eye of our ultimate ancestor came into existence on a solid foundation of knowledge about the inner and outer worlds necessary for living in this spatial universe.

(Applause) If you elevate this question one step higher and ask, "God, will you be the God and Father of all people, or will you be the God and Father bound to a Christian denomination?" He will surely respond, "Oh, even if I cannot be the God of a Christian denomination, I will be the God of all people." He will undoubtedly answer like that. (Applause)  
From this perspective, we are currently in a historical chaos where we must once again critically examine everything centered on theism, humanism, and materialism, and seek a way to re-evaluate the world from God's standpoint. This is the task of religion. It is the responsibility of religious leaders. Until now, they have been fighting over denominations without knowing what God's will is. Let me introduce you to a memorable verse from the Bible. This is a verse that even Sunday school students or kindergarteners know well. In John 3:16, it says, "For God so loved the world that He gave His only begotten Son, that whoever believes in Him should not perish but have everlasting life." It is important to recognize that God gave His only begotten Son because He loved the world, not because He loved the church.  
We have not known the standard of world salvation until now. The established churches did not know this standard and stood on a position of ecclesiastical authoritarianism, breaking down the good foundation of the Middle Ages that could encompass the world. Even today, if we look at the United States, if the church that led the democratic world had known that it was God's will to embrace the United States and save the world, and had fought with that momentum, the United States would not have ended up as miserable as it is today.  
Everyone, let us not be discouraged by the difficulties of our Republic of Korea. Even if we are struggling, it is okay. No matter how much we are at the peak of material civilization and in a position of a leading global nation, looking at the United States itself, there is no place to put our affection. When someone asks me, "Mr. Moon, would you like to live in America?" I say I do not want to live in America. That is why I miss the Korean people who can worry about their neighbors while sweating and eating gochujang. They can still struggle toward the future and have hope for tomorrow, but they are all liberated. They have reached a saturation point. Everyone, do not despair. Do not despair.  
You are all aware of the historical fact that the Soviet Union, centered on the Slavic people, dreamed of dominating world communism and began to split around 1957. If God exists, we must think that individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world are needed to save the world. Citizens of the Republic of Korea gathered here, our nation may have nothing, but if we can carry a higher dimension of heart that can serve beyond our nation to the world, then perhaps our Republic of Korea itself may lack strength, but because of the omnipotent God who exists as the subject of that principle, I firmly believe that we will one day become a nation that the world can serve. **New Hope for Humanity**  
― Message from the Hope Day Grand Gathering in Gwangju ―  
I sincerely thank the citizens of Gwangju for gathering here this evening. I also sincerely apologize to the many citizens of Gwangju who could not attend due to the cramped venue and are outside.  
It is not very exciting to listen to these stiff words while you are enjoying good songs, dances, and interesting programs. However, when you see the scene of foreign young men and women suddenly coming in and causing unrest in the quiet city of Gwangju over these past few days, you must have been quite curious about who the person responsible for this issue, Mr. Moon, is.  
The very person responsible, Moon Sun-myung, has appeared here. I may not be very good-looking, but beloved citizens of Gwangju, (Applause) I love Gwangju. Why do I love it? It is not because you are applauding me. The character “Gwangju” consists of the characters for “light” (光) and “district” (州), meaning a shining district. Therefore, if I can make a name for myself in Gwangju, it will resonate throughout the nation, and I believe that all things must start wonderfully from Gwangju. Thus, I love the name Gwangju and the citizens of Gwangju.  
For this reason, this evening, I would like to briefly share my thoughts with you. The title I wish to think about with you this evening is “New Hope for Humanity” or “New Aspirations for Humanity.” I will speak on this topic.  
**Seeking a New Future Through God**  
As you all know, the world we live in is chaotic. We are facing a present filled with fear and despair. If we cannot find new hope or new aspirations in such a world, and if a new guiding ideology or a central thought sought by all humanity does not emerge, then a new future and a new world of hope cannot manifest.  
As you well know, since the Middle Ages, the decline of uncertain theocentric ideologies has swept the world with humanism. Following the decline of humanism, materialism, or what we call materialistic ideologies, has engulfed the world, but rather than bringing hope, it has increased despair and fear. When we look at this fact, humanity is indeed facing a whirlpool of despair.  
When we consider why these historical ideologies have fallen into decay and stagnation, it is not because humans have made mistakes. We humans have made every effort and have invested all our intelligence and abilities, yet we find ourselves in a world of such results and are now in a state of despair where we cannot move forward or backward. Here, if we raise one question, it is that we can no longer seek a new future for humanity without relying on something beyond humanity. This conclusion is reasonable.  
If there is a central being that can solve this conclusion, that being must be God. Is there a definite existence of God? If God certainly exists, what is the original view of God, what is God's view of humanity, and what is God's view of the material world? These are all issues that can be clearly elucidated. Therefore, it is not an exaggeration to conclude that we have reached this result because we have not clearly realized whether God exists or not.  
As you all know, today, intellectuals are debating whether thought comes first or existence comes first. This has become a philosophical issue. Does thought come first, or does existence come first? The issue of thought, followed by the issue of existence, whether it is spirit or matter, and then whether it is God or creation—these fundamental questions remain unresolved, and we are facing the reality of wandering in confusion.  
Therefore, now we must ask, is there a God? If there is something that can provide evidence for God, then if the citizens of Gwangju here can gather and say, “Ah, surely He exists,” it is undeniable that Gwangju can become the vanguard of inspiring a new ideology in the world.  
**Proving God's Reality Through the Human Body**  
Now, how can I give an impressive example to the citizens of Gwangju here and help you find “an example that you cannot forget, day or night”? I have thought about this. Since many elderly people are present here, it is difficult to express this simply, but I hope you will remember one example.  
Among our body parts, the eyes are important. By looking into someone's eyes, you can understand their heart, right? “That person has beautiful eyes,” and so on. The eyes are also called the light of the heart. Now, if we look closely at the eyes and ask them, “Hey, eyes! Why are you like this? Where did you come from?” they would surely answer, “Where did I come from? I came through my mom and dad.” That is undoubtedly how they would respond. Then if we ask, “Where did your mom and dad's eyes come from?” they would say, “Where do you think they came from? They came from my grandparents and so on….” So, they were born from their ancestors' eyes, but the eyes themselves are material.  
When the eyes are born, do they know that “if I am born on Earth, there is a sun”? This is a simple question. Would they know that? The eyes themselves cannot know. When we ask whether the eyes knew that there was a sun in the sky, the answer is that they cannot know. Do you think they knew? I see a student smiling. The eyes themselves could not know whether there was a sun in the sky before the Earth appeared. They cannot know that.  
Next, if we think about the eyes, they would not have known about the sun, but when water evaporates due to radiant heat, it would be a disaster, so they would need to create a mechanism to prevent evaporation and blink their eyes. Would the eyes themselves know that? Think about it carefully. The eyes themselves would not know, “Ah, in this air….” Can you see water vapor? You cannot, right? Ah, you know that if the moisture in the eyes dries up due to the evaporation of water, it would be a disaster. Try not blinking for about 30 minutes and see what happens to your eyes. It would be a disaster.  
When the eyes are born, do they know that “water vapor evaporates in the air”? If someone says they knew, that person is a bit strange. They are somewhat lacking in understanding. That’s fine. Not knowing is the case for everyone. Furthermore, if we look a step further, you have eyelashes on your eyes. There are springs there. What were they thinking when they were created? When the eyes were born, did they say, “In the air, because the air flows and dust exists, my eyes, you should have eyelashes”? No one would say they knew that. The conclusion that they did not know is obvious. If someone claims they knew, that person is somewhat lacking in understanding.  
Moreover, when we examine our bodies, we find a palace of mysteries. Everything is beautifully arranged. Among them, when the eyes are born, they are synchronized with the place where the sun is, and they are arranged to prevent the evaporation of water, and they are aware of the dust in the air and are designed to prevent it. The fact that they can observe the solar system of the universe and know about the phenomenon of evaporation in the air, and that they know there is dust in the flowing air, leads us to think that although the eyes themselves do not know, there is someone who knows these facts and has allowed the eyes to exist based on biological knowledge. When we look at it this way, it is an undeniable conclusion that there is a subject who thought of this, even if the eyes themselves did not think.  
When we first think about this, we see that there was a motivational knowledge base that allowed for such an environment to be created. Then, who is the subject of that knowledge? The name does not matter. It could be a rock or a stone. In Japanese, it is called kami (かみ), in Korean, it is called 하나님, and in English, it is called God. The name does not matter. We cannot deny that there was some kind of biological protagonist.  
You know, why are there so many eye doctors in the world, including in Gwangju? There are many here, but if we look at the world, there are hundreds of thousands of eye doctors, but have those doctors completely uncovered the mysteries of the eyes and found knowledge that explains everything? They have not. Therefore, from this perspective of cosmic biology, we cannot deny that there was a fundamental reason, spirit, and thought that allowed the eyes to exist. Every morning when you wash your face and look at your eyes, think about this. They knew how to stand and walk. They should not sweat…  
Also, wouldn’t it be nice if the nose were upside down? Why is it wide like this? Because if you sweat, it would be a disaster. They created a channel so that sweat could flow away… When we see that everything is known and has come to be, we cannot think that matter existed first and then this happened. I hope you understand that the origin of spirit and thought had a fundamental motivational starting point. Therefore, I wanted to convey that “God must exist. He is here.”  
Thus, there is God in the universe; this being exists. If we have realized that God exists, we must know about God. That God cannot desire for this human world to be as it is. Because He is higher, holier, better, and more loving than us, it is only natural that He wants to bring true love, ideals, happiness, peace, and freedom to this human world.  
**God's True Ideals, Love, Peace, and Happiness Through Humanity**  
So how can we humans meet the ideal requirements that He demands? Humans have always pursued true and unchanging love, ideals, peace, happiness, and freedom, but now we have all hit dead ends and find ourselves in a state where we cannot have hope, and we are in despair, lamenting not only ourselves but also the world.  
From here, we must discover a new path that transcends human nature, returning to an unchanging subject, God, so that a new guiding ideology and a new central thought can manifest a new future and a world of hope.  
God and we humans are hoping for true ideals, true love, true peace, and true happiness. When will this ideal world, the world of love, the world of happiness, and the world of peace be realized? It will be when the two become one.  
Then what is the issue here? Should God come down to meet the standards we humans desire, or should we humans rise to meet Him?  
When we consider who the subject is and who the object is, it must be that God is the subject. We must discover humanity that can be unified according to the requirements that God, as the subject, demands. Thus, we must engage in the play of reshaping humanity to that standard; otherwise, true love, true ideals, true peace, and true happiness that God desires cannot be established with us humans. This is an obvious conclusion.  
Therefore, you must now follow what God presents. The issue here is that God is the subject and we humans are the object. Then, when we question whether true love, true happiness, and true peace are terms that can exist alone, the answer is that they cannot exist alone. When we speak of love, it must be established in recognizing the relationship between subject and object. Can there be peace alone? There must be a relationship between subject and object. Can there be an ideal alone? There cannot be an ideal alone. There must also be a relationship between subject and object. And happiness cannot exist alone either; we must understand this here. These terms are always determined in the relationship between subject and object.  
Thus, if we present an issue, it is that to achieve God's true love, God's ideals, God's happiness, and God's peace, there must be an object; otherwise, God cannot do it either. What can God do if He says, “Ah, let’s love” and loves alone? What can God do if He has ideals alone? What can God do if He has peace or happiness alone? There must be an object for God to also need happiness, peace, love, and ideals.
