Heaven is a place where only those who exist for the sake of others can enter and live. It’s simple. (Applause) 

How do you determine whether you can go to heaven or hell? Those who live for themselves will surely go to hell. However, those who deny themselves and live for the sake of the whole, for the sake of others, will surely go to heaven. Even if someone believes in Jesus well, if they are self-centered, no matter how well they believe, they cannot go to heaven. However, I have met many conscientious people who do not believe in Jesus but are willing to live for the world and follow the laws of justice, and they have gone to higher spiritual realms than those who believe well in Jesus. (Applause) Ah, there are laws in the world; can the heavenly kingdom be run arbitrarily? No, it cannot.

Today, citizens of Gwangju, remember one thing after meeting a person named Moon this evening: "Those who go to heaven are those who live for the sake of others." Heaven is where God resides, so the heavenly kingdom is our homeland. Humans are travelers. You must understand that the life of this traveler is to pass through the sunset road and the night world to reach their eternal path.

If humans had not originally fallen, they would have inherited the tradition of living for the sake of others and would have formed this world into a peaceful world, a heavenly kingdom on earth. However, they have explored the path of self-centered discovery, which is the fall.

In order for fallen humans to return to their homeland, God must train them to align with the laws of the heavenly kingdom. That training ground is what we call religion. This varies by ethnicity. Because the ethnic background, cultural background, or customary background is different, through suitable forms of religion, like a river flowing toward a great ocean, we must understand that a providence is being carried out that leads to one sea. Today, Christianity claims that "there is no salvation outside of Christianity," but the world I know is not like that. In the spiritual world, I have seen Jesus and Buddha together. I have seen Confucius as well; they are all like that. You must understand this.

The place that trains people to be able to find the path to that heavenly homeland is religion, so those who believe in religion must follow the tradition of living for the sake of others. There is no tradition of living for oneself. The higher the religion, the more it emphasizes sacrifice and service, and we have not understood why this is the case theoretically. Why must it be so? Because religion does not suit the tastes of young people, as they are fallen humans. The laws of the heavenly homeland are like that. Therefore, in order to align fallen humans with that law, God, who is love, must provide the highest training. This principle must be established that one should not go the path of death for oneself but should go for the sake of others. That is why it is said to be gentle and humble, to sacrifice and serve. When the day comes when your life unfolds in a way that can live for a broader stage, the city of Gwangju will be directed toward a good direction because of you, and when that extends beyond the nation to the world, this nation will develop into a world of eternal goodness. I hope you remember this one thing as you return. (Applause)

If we conclude this, today, those who do not believe in our religion might say, "What? When a person dies, that’s it. Like a puff of smoke, it all disappears. What is life then…." But that is not true. If that were the case, I would not be doing this work while being opposed all my life. Do you think I am doing this work because I am less than you? The world may say whatever, but I know that the path I must take in life is the path of destiny, so I must hurry along that path. If a new guest passes by, the neighborhood dogs bark. Isn’t that so? That’s not the issue; it’s that my path is busy, so our Unification Church has come this far like a mute.

God is eternal, absolute, and unique, and He desires humans to be the same. You must understand that God is eternal, God is absolute, and God is unique. When we say that humans are the sons of His love and exist as objects of love, would God want humans to exist for a moment and then disappear? People in our world feel the same way, don’t they? "Oh, my beloved will be forever…. You are my eternal love…." Whether in poetry, literature, or in closing our eyes or opening them, we wish for eternity. Right? Even humans living in this world desire that the object of love, the ideal or the object of happiness, be eternal. How would God feel?

After meeting the son whom He can love, would God say, "Hey, I am eternal, but you should live for about a hundred years and then die. Disappear!"? That cannot be. 

In front of the subject God, the Father God, humans who are to be His sons and daughters must remember that since the Father is eternal, it is a theoretical conclusion that the children must also live eternally. (Applause) Are you really happy? Here you are clapping, but later this evening, you might say, "Well, that sounds good, but let’s wait and see." Please don’t do that. It’s not right for people to clap here and then change when they go back. I know that the people of Gwangju are honest, so please don’t do that.

Now, having understood this, you have a general understanding. Apply this formula. When you want to make friends, what kind of friend do you want? Someone who gives for your sake, right? Isn’t that so? If it’s a country, you want a country that exists for your sake, right? That’s for sure. We naturally like those who exist for our sake, and since we like that, God, who resembles us, also likes those who exist for His sake. I hope you remember this.

Now, why could God not help but establish the law of existing for the sake of others? 

Then, among you, some might say, "Well, that’s good. That law of existing for the sake of others is good, but what about God?" Young people might feel uncomfortable thinking like this. They might say, "We have fought with all our might, eyes wide open, and clenched our fists, but we are told to exist for the sake of others? Don’t say such foolish things. The world is different now." But that is not the case.

So, let’s discuss why the God of wisdom had to establish the law of existing for the sake of others by presenting a few conditions. I want to ask you a question. If there is someone who has invested their entire life for me, making me owe them 100 percent, would you want to repay only 50 percent and keep the other 50 percent for yourself? Or would you want to repay more than 100 percent? Which is it? The latter, right? I am the latter. What about you? You are the latter too, right? "Yes." You resemble me. I resemble you, and you resemble me. It is definitely the latter.

When we receive the grace of life, there is a desire in our nature to want to give back more, which is why humanity can develop into a world of hope. True humanity.
The fact that meeting each other can become a motivation for infinite development is something we need to understand here. (Applause) So, if I loved a person named B and devoted my life to them, and if this person B were to repay me with 100 percent of that devotion, I would think, "Oh, that's great! I received more, so I made a good deal." Is that right? My true intention would be to say, "The gratitude I received is a debt, so give me more." 

Therefore, if I invested 100 percent of my devotion and received 110 percent in return, I would want to give back more than 110 percent, and this kind of play would occur. This kind of play only exists in the context of giving and receiving. As a result, we did not realize that the concept of eternity is established here. (Applause) The concept of eternity was born here. From this point, eternal life, and from this place, eternity... Therefore, love, ideals, happiness, and peace must be eternal. Also, because it starts from here, I hope you remember that God, who becomes the king of wisdom, could not help but establish the principle of existence for the sake of others. (Applause)

Moreover, we did not realize that the concept of eternity being established simultaneously means that development and prosperity exist only here. (Applause) Did you understand that? First, eternity is established here, and prosperity exists here, for the sake of others.

Next, what is the second point? You know, right? Nowadays, if young people are dominated by others, they would be in a state of hunger and pain, almost to the point of dying. Right? Isn't that so? There are students here. I’m saying don’t be like that. Listen to me. They really dislike being dominated, but if someone says, "Be dominated," they want to resist and say, "What is this?" They wait a little. But they dislike that too, right? They dislike it, but they are told to wait.

In the so-called clubs of intelligent people who think they are smart these days, there are many such people. "Wow, who can I lose to? The prestige of a university professor, the prestige of a president..." It’s a big deal. But that’s not how it is.

Up until now, being ruled and dominated by others has been seen as an insult, a failure, and something unfair. However, we have never thought about the happiness of being able to be dominated by someone who can truly care for us. (Applause)

Let’s see if that’s true or not. Let’s say there are eight family members living in one household. Among those eight, let’s say there is a little younger sibling who is in their 20s. Even though there are many older siblings and both parents, if this younger sibling cares for the family more than anyone else, day or night, more than their mother or father, what happens? The longer they care, the more they do not get kicked out of the house, but rather, they gradually take the central position. We cannot help but think that there is such a principle. (Applause) The younger sibling, who cares more than the older siblings and the mother, will eventually be recognized by the parents and older siblings as the one who can inherit the family. 

What kind of person should the mayor of Gwangju be? They should be someone who cares for Gwangju more than anyone else. If they act like a parent for all the citizens of Gwangju day and night, the citizens will gradually... even if that person does not want to be the mayor, they will be made the mayor. Right? (Applause) Isn’t that so? "Yes, it is."

Parents treat their children, whether it's Gabdol or Oksoon, saying, "Do good things." "What is a good thing, mom and dad?" When they ask, "Well, I don’t know, but when someone is hungry, feed them, and when they fall, pick them up, that’s all for the sake of others." That’s the only thing they say. Isn’t that so? Then they think they will become good, but they didn’t know the specifics. These smart young people... 

When you look at the content of the scriptures, it seems like a paradoxical logic, but when you realize that the ideal creation of the universe started from the principle of caring for others, it fits perfectly. Look at the Bible from this perspective. When you think about it, if you have wisdom, you will discover that Jesus is indeed the savior of humanity. (Applause)

Now, time is passing, and it’s almost time to wrap up. Should I stop here, or should I conclude a little more? "Keep going." Okay, I will.

So, now you know the secret that living for others leads to becoming a central being. Try living for your school. You receive awards and become representatives of the entire school. Right? Because the origin of the universal principle is set up that way, we did not realize that without aligning with that origin, the value of existence cannot be formed. The one who lives for others becomes a central being. Why? Because they resemble God. Do you understand? Because they resemble God. (Applause)

The God who is the center of the universe exists according to the principle of caring for others since the creation. Nowadays, people say God is dead, and they wonder, "Does that God even exist? Whatever you say..." But still, God forgives and cares for others, so those who live for others resemble God. Therefore, just as God is the center of the universe, the longer we live, the more we will emerge as central beings, and now everyone understands this logical principle. So, I hope you live that way.

Next, there is no greater happiness than being dominated by someone who lives for others. Do you understand what that means? Try being dominated by someone who lives for others. When a husband works for his wife, the wife, not knowing where to put her body, just asks, "Bring me food." Even if she wants water, she doesn’t have to say it; he will bring it to her, right? That’s right. I’m not a woman, but I know that’s true. So, we did not realize how amazing this happiness is, being able to be completely dominated by someone who lives for others.

God is the central being of the universe who lives for others, so when we get close to Him, even if we are dominated for a thousand years, we want to be dominated even more. Because the principle of caring for others is established around God, if we can be dominated in such a position today, we have never even thought about the fact that there is no greater happiness than that.

Now, the third reason is, why could God not help but establish the law of living for others? Let’s talk about it. Nowadays, both men and women, those who think they are great, have thought, "If I love, it’s my love; if I have ideals, it’s my ideals!" But that’s not it. Love cannot be obtained alone. Ideals cannot be achieved alone. They are obtained in a relative relationship. Love does not come from me. Ideals do not come from me. The love and ideals that are more precious than life come not from me but from the other party, so to receive these precious things, one must humbly care for others. That’s why I hope you understand that the principle of caring for others must be established. (Applause)

Now, I believe you have understood a lot. "Ah, I see!" This eye was not born because of the eye. It was for the other party. The ear was not born because of the ear. Everything... The nose was not born because of the nose. The mouth was not born because of the mouth. It was born because of the other party. The arm was born because of the arm? It was for others. Everything is like that. Now, if you understand that much, let’s move on. 

The Method of Religious Unification and God’s Will
"Now, who is this Moon, and what is he doing to cause a stir in this world and in South Korea?" In Christianity, there are many people who fervently pray, "Oh, I wish that Moon would die." But I won’t die. If those who wish for my death die, then they die, but I won’t die. I’m living plump and healthy. Why won’t I die? Because I follow the principle of heaven. Those who strike someone following the principle of heaven will hit themselves. "Can you, the founder of the Unification Church, unify religions and Christianity?" They will say that.

When people hear the name Unification Church, those with good heads might criticize it. "Isn’t that Moon a bit of a fool?" they might interpret it simply, but just wait a moment. The old church and the new church, the Roman Catholic Church and the Greek Orthodox Church have been divided for 950 years, and nowadays they want to become one, but can they? Even among the new churches, there are over 400 denominations fighting, saying, "If it’s not my denomination, there is no God." How can they become one? They cannot.

How can they become one? According to what Master Moon of the Unification Church says, it can be done. When I call myself Master Moon, it’s not appropriate. But all the members of the Unification Church call me Master Moon, so I’m calling it out. It means to follow what Moon says.

How does it work? If I, as a Catholic, care for God, then I will care for God. "As long as the Catholic Church cares for the Lord, I will care for them, and as long as the priests and nuns care for the church members, I will love them." What do you think will happen? (Applause) People will want to be loved more and cared for more, even if they have to drag their necks or even if their necks are cut off. This is the desire of our nature. When I love the members of the established church more than the established church pastors, we can become one. When the members of the established church stand in a position where they can care for the established church pastors more than the established church pastors care for their members, it will simply become unified. Is that right? (Applause) Is that right? "Yes, it is."

Look at this. What is God’s will? What is God’s will? "If it’s Presbyterian, it’s for the Presbyterians; if it’s Methodist, it’s for the Methodists to take to heaven." That’s how they would answer, right? If you ask what God’s will is through Master Moon of the Unification Church, they might say, "If you listen to Moon, you will go to heaven. That’s God’s will." But I don’t say that. What is God’s will? God wants to love more than Presbyterians, Methodists, Holiness churches, and the Unification Church, and He wants to care for humanity more. What is God’s will? It is not to take Presbyterians to heaven. It is not to take the Holiness Church to heaven. It is not to take the Unification Church to heaven. Then what is it? It is to take humanity to heaven, which many sects today do not know. They do not know. (Applause)

God wants to save humanity even if it means sacrificing the Presbyterians. That is God’s will. "Save humanity even if it means sacrificing the Holiness Church." This is God’s demand. "Save humanity even if it means sacrificing the Methodists." That is God’s will. "Even if it means sacrificing the Unification Church a hundred or a thousand times, even if it means being persecuted, saving humanity is better than any religion." (Applause)

Today, we do not realize that the time has come to tear down the walls of existing religions. What is God’s will? I have come to know that it is not just to take the established church to heaven.

Christianity does not know God’s will to save the world.
If there are Christian believers here, I would like to ask one thing. If you were to ask the Lord whom you respect and believe in with all your heart, "Lord, is your desire for me to live only for Christianity, for Presbyterians, or is it your will to live for the sake of humanity even if it means abandoning Presbyterianism?" there would be Presbyterian pastors here. Which is God’s will? Is it only to live for Presbyterians? You should live that way.

However, even if it means stepping over Presbyterians, it is the responsibility of religion to strive to save humanity, which they did not realize. If you ask the Lord, "Do you want to be the Lord of Christianity or the Lord of humanity?" He would want to be the Lord of humanity. He would want to be the Lord of humanity. (Applause)

When we elevate the question to God, "Is your will only to save Christianity?" God would answer, "No. My will is to embrace all fallen lives. I have a heart that desires to find the lost children like a parent and a subject that longs to love my ideal partner. My will is to save all humanity." This is the position that today’s Roman Catholic Church and Christianity around the world do not know. (Applause)

Today, the Unification Church has been persecuted in South Korea for 30 years. However, I said, "Father, if South Korea can be blessed by my persecution, then I am willing to suffer as much as necessary. Even if the established church curses me, I will pray and go in the position of caring for God and the established church." Let’s see what happens in the end. In the end, who will remain? Those who opposed will disappear, and those who were opposed can become the owners. Many established church members do not think about this. They think sadly about this.

If you do not believe that, let me give you an example from a well-known verse in the Bible. From kindergarten or elementary school, in Sunday school, there is a well-known verse. In John 3:16, it says, "For God so loved the world that He gave His only begotten Son, that whoever believes in Him should not perish but have everlasting life." He gave His only begotten Son because He loved the world, not just Christianity. It is not just for Presbyterians. It is not just for the Unification Church. It is God’s will to save the world, and they do not know the Lord’s will. Can you call it a heresy or a cult? (Applause)

In this untrustworthy world where the fake looks real and the real looks fake, I had a desire not to want to return to this South Korea that curses the Unification Church. However, because I was born as a son of Korea, even if my bones melt and my flesh withers, I cannot just trample on the spirit of the nation that our ancestors left behind. When I think of South Korea, which should have hope for the future, even if it is a South Korea that opposes me, I want to take a step to care for this country as much as possible, gathering the youth from around the world. I hope you remember that today is a great celebration of hope. (Applause)

Christianity has a responsibility to save the world. Communism, of course, and the democratic world also have the responsibility to capture everything and lead it to God, yet they have weakened and lost not only their purpose but even their current position and are wandering. What good is it to wait for the Lord to return tomorrow? That will not fulfill His will.
Can you follow along? It requires training. That is why our Unification Church lives for the sake of others; only there can it become heaven. If individuals can live for the sake of the world, transcending nations and overcoming East and West, and transcending races, then that place becomes a personal heaven that encompasses the world. If families do so, then family heaven will be realized. If nations do so, then national heaven will be realized. If the world does so, then we have not even begun to think about the formation of national heaven and world heaven on this earth. (Applause)

The path the Unification Church is taking
So today, although people say various things about the Unification Church, when they see the establishment of the Victory Alliance, they think, “Ah, the Unification Church is just a means for evangelism…” Not at all. It is because we anticipated how this country should move forward that we are doing this work, even if this nation and this people do not realize it. We have made tremendous sacrifices. By sacrificing the Unification Church, we are paving the way for the nation and the people to move forward; by sacrificing the members of the Unification Church today, we are paving the way for humanity to move forward. We are working day and night, tirelessly, to expand the heavenly realm even by an inch, and there must be at least one person in some corner of this planet who is doing this. (Applause)

Heaven desires to establish one individual, one family, one tribe, and one nation, and to seek the way to one world based on a transnational heart. This is the ideology of this man who stands here and has heard many accusations of heresy and various rumors. I would appreciate it if you could believe this.

A new hope for humanity
(Applause)
Everyone, you are well aware of the Vietnam situation. In light of North Korea's current intentions to invade the South, Christianity cannot remain solely as Christianity. The time has come to unite with the nation.

When you fight, you must unite and fight without distinguishing between the Unification Church and Christianity. If Christianity fights and fails, we must join the fight and contribute to the path of victory. In this urgent and critical time, citizens of Gwangju, we must unite here. We must unite and carry a higher-level ideology for a unified nation, and to crush evil… On the day we can unite with the mindset that I can offer my life as a sacrifice before heaven, this nation will not be a nation of misfortune. There is no reason for us to lose to North Korea, whether in population or in any other aspect.

That is why I am laying the groundwork in Japan, in the United States, and blocking the actions of the global evil to unify world Christianity for the victory of God. We must understand that it is the mission of Christianity and what God requires of us to save even the communists through strength. (Applause)

Let us advance for the sake of others
From this perspective, the time has come for a progressive formal process and the establishment of a new paradigm. The issue is not how to establish an individual’s view of life. The question is how individuals, based on that view, will form a national view, a worldview, and a cosmic view. It is not about that. Only through the progressive path that exists for the sake of others can a single world be formed, where all ideal conditions can be established from the higher dimension of heaven.

Therefore, an individual man exists for the sake of his wife, that couple exists for the sake of their children, that family exists for the sake of the tribe, the tribe exists for the sake of the nation, the nation exists for the sake of the world, the world exists for the sake of God, and only then does God finally exist for our sake… Following this principle of a world that exists for the sake of others resolves the individual’s view of life, the national view, the worldview, and the view of God’s providence. If this foundation can extend throughout the world, even to the communist world, and if that world can truly become one, then indeed, God will send all seekers and the Savior to fulfill the purpose of saving the world, completing the heavenly kingdom on earth, and I hope you all believe this. (Applause)

For the sake of a higher dimension, South Korea must now find how to establish a South Korea that can serve Asia from the time it serves itself and how to establish a South Korea that can serve a higher dimension of the world. Even if South Korea is currently lagging in all aspects and is in a position of underdevelopment, that is not a problem. In the 23rd century or the 25th century, when we understand how to serve, the ideal standard that all people will need can be globally proclaimed, and on the day we lay the groundwork, we may be experiencing difficulties now, but in two or three centuries, we will become a leading nation that can guide the world. We have understood this principle. (Applause)

The same goes for the church. The church must also follow this principle. If it only serves its denomination, it will be judged because of that denomination. It will perish because of that denomination. We have come to understand that we must walk the path of serving God’s will and humanity.

Today, we have desires for ownership in everything. In conclusion, I want to say that now what belongs to the wife is mine, what is mine is the wife’s, and what belongs to the parents is for the children. What belongs to the family is not just for the family. It must become a society that can connect what belongs to the tribe. What belongs to the tribe is for the nation. What belongs to the nation is not just the property of South Korea, which stands in a decisive position within its own borders. It must become property that can connect to the world. What belongs to South Korea is for the world, and what belongs to the world is for God. Only then can we say, “What belongs to God is truly mine.” This is how the thick, toad-like greed of humanity can be satisfied. Then, what belongs to God is mine. (Applause)

This new subject ideology, which prevents the downfall of individuals with ambiguous centers, prevents the downfall of society, prevents a nation without a center, prevents a world without a center, and prevents a providence of God without a center, is the only formal trajectory that starts from the principle of existing for the sake of others and remains eternally from the world of God’s creation to the final destination. Please remember this, and after attending today, I hope there will be higher-level development and innovation in that regard as I conclude my remarks.

I wish blessings upon your families, your societies, and your Gwangju, and I hope you remain well as I take my leave. (Applause)
